<a name="rtr"></a>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-399">路由範本參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-399">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-400">內 `{}` 的權杖會定義路由參數，這些參數會在路由相符時系結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-400">Tokens within `{}` define route parameters that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-401">路由區段中可以定義一個以上的路由參數，但路由參數必須以常值分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-401">More than one route parameter can be defined in a route segment, but route parameters  must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-402">例如，`{controller=Home}{action=Index}` 不是有效的路由，因為 `{controller}` 與 `{action}` 之間沒有任何常值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-402">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-403">路由參數必須有名稱，而且可能會指定其他屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-403">Route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-404">路由參數之外的常值文字 (例如，`{id}`) 和路徑分隔符號 `/` 必須符合 URL 中的文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-404">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-405">文字比對不區分大小寫，而且會根據 URL 路徑的已解碼標記法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-405">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URL's path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-406">若要比對常值路由參數分隔符號 `{` 或 `}` ，請重複字元來將分隔符號取消。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-406">To match a literal route parameter delimiter `{` or `}`, escape the delimiter by repeating the character.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-407">例如， `{{` 或 `}}` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-407">For example `{{` or `}}`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-408">星號 `*` 或雙星號 `**` ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-408">Asterisk `*` or double asterisk `**`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-409">可以用來作為路由參數的前置詞，以系結至 URI 的其餘部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-409">Can be used as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-410">稱為 **全部攔截** 參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-410">Are called a **catch-all** parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-411">例如，`blog/{**slug}`：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-411">For example, `blog/{**slug}`:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-412">比對以開頭的任何 URI， `/blog` 並在後面加上任何值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-412">Matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-413">下列值 `/blog` 會指派給 [資訊](https://developer.mozilla.org/docs/Glossary/Slug) 區路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-413">The value following `/blog` is assigned to the [slug](https://developer.mozilla.org/docs/Glossary/Slug) route value.</span></span>

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/catchall.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-414">全部擷取參數也可以符合空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-414">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-415">當使用路由來產生 URL （包括路徑分隔符號）時，全部攔截參數會將適當的字元進行轉義 `/` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-415">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator `/` characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-416">例如，路由值為 `{ path = "my/path" }` 的路由 `foo/{*path}` 會產生 `foo/my%2Fpath`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-416">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-417">請注意逸出的斜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-417">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-418">若要反覆存取路徑分隔符號字元，請使用 `**` 路由參數前置詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-418">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-419">具有 `{ path = "my/path" }` 的路由 `foo/{**path}` 會產生 `foo/my/path`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-419">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-420">URL 模式嘗試擷取具有選擇性副檔名的檔案名稱時，具有其他考量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-420">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-421">以範本 `files/{filename}.{ext?}` 為例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-421">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-422">當 `filename` 和 `ext` 都存在值時，就會填入這兩個值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-422">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-423">如果 `filename` URL 中只有存在的值，則路由會相符，因為尾端 `.` 是選擇性的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-423">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing `.` is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-424">下列 URL 符合此路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-424">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-425">路由參數可能有「預設值」，指定方法是在參數名稱之後指定預設值，並以等號 (`=`) 分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-425">Route parameters may have **default values** designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-426">例如，`{controller=Home}` 定義 `Home` 作為 `controller` 的預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-426">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-427">如果 URL 中沒有用於參數的任何值，則會使用預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-427">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-428">路由參數是選擇性的，方法是將問號 (`?`) 附加到參數名稱的結尾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-428">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-429">例如： `id?` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-429">For example, `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-430">選擇性值與預設路由參數之間的差異如下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-430">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-431">具有預設值的路由參數一定會產生值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-431">A route parameter with a default value always produces a value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-432">選擇性參數只有在要求 URL 提供值時才會有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-432">An optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-433">路由參數可能具有條件約束，這些條件約束必須符合與 URL 繫結的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-433">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-434">在 `:` 路由參數名稱之後加入和條件約束名稱，會在路由參數上指定內嵌條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-434">Adding `:` and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an inline constraint on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-435">如果條件約束需要引數，這些引數會在條件約束名稱後面以括弧 `(...)` 括住。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-435">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses `(...)` after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-436">您可以附加另一個和條件約束名稱，以指定多個 *內嵌條件約束* `:` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-436">Multiple *inline constraints* can be specified by appending another `:` and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-437">條件約束名稱和引述會傳遞至 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> 服務來建立 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 的執行個體，以用於 URL 處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-437">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-438">例如，路由範本 `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` 指定具有引數 `10` 的 `minlength` 條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-438">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-439">如需路由條件約束詳細資訊和架構所提供的條件約束清單，請參閱[路由條件約束參考](#route-constraint-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-439">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-440">路由參數也可以具有參數轉換器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-440">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-441">參數轉換程式會在產生連結並比對動作和頁面至 Url 時，轉換參數的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-441">Parameter transformers transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-442">如同條件約束，您可以在 `:` 路由參數名稱之後加入和轉換程式名稱，以內嵌方式將參數轉換器新增至路由參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-442">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a `:` and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-443">例如，路由範本 `blog/{article:slugify}` 會指定 `slugify` 轉換器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-443">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-444">如需參數轉換器的詳細資訊，請參閱[參數轉器參考](#parameter-transformer-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-444">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-445">下表示范範例路由範本及其行為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-445">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-446">路由範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-446">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-447">範例比對 URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-447">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-448">要求 URI&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-448">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-449">只比對單一路徑 `/hello`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-449">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-450">比對並將 `Page` 設定為 `Home`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-450">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-451">比對並將 `Page` 設定為 `Contact`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-451">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-452">對應至 `Products` 控制器和 `List` 動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-452">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-453">會對應至 `Products`  `Details` 設定為123的控制器和動作 `id` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-453">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action with`id` set to 123.</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-454">對應至 `Home` 控制器和 `Index` 方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-454">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-455">已忽略 `id`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-455">`id` is ignored.</span></span>        |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/Products`         | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-456">對應至 `Products` 控制器和 `Index` 方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-456">Maps to the `Products` controller and `Index` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-457">已忽略 `id`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-457">`id` is ignored.</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-458">使用範本通常是最簡單的路由方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-458">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-459">條件約束和預設值也可以在路由範本外部指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-459">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

### <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-460">複雜區段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-460">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-461">複雜區段的處理方式是在 [非貪婪](#greedy) 的情況下，由右至左比對常值分隔符號。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-461">Complex segments are processed by matching up literal delimiters from right to left in a [non-greedy](#greedy) way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-462">例如， `[Route("/a{b}c{d}")]` 是複雜區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-462">For example, `[Route("/a{b}c{d}")]` is a complex segment.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-463">複雜的區段會以特定的方式運作，必須瞭解才能成功使用它們。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-463">Complex segments work in a particular way that must be understood to use them successfully.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-464">本章節中的範例會示範當分隔符號文字未出現在參數值內部時，複雜區段只會很適合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-464">The example in this section demonstrates why complex segments only really work well when the delimiter text doesn't appear inside the parameter values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-465">使用 [RegEx](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expressions) ，然後以手動方式將值解壓縮，對較複雜的案例而言是必要的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-465">Using a [regex](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expressions) and then manually extracting the values is needed for more complex cases.</span></span>

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/regex.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-466">這是路由使用範本和 URL 路徑執行的步驟摘要 `/a{b}c{d}` `/abcd` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-466">This is a summary of the steps that routing performs with the template `/a{b}c{d}` and the URL path `/abcd`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-467">`|`用來協助視覺化演算法的運作方式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-467">The `|` is used to help visualize how the algorithm works:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-468">第一個常值（由右至左）為 `c` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-468">The first literal, right to left, is `c`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-469">這 `/abcd` 會從右側搜尋並尋找 `/ab|c|d` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-469">So `/abcd` is searched from right and finds `/ab|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-470">右邊 () 的所有內容 `d` 現在都會與 route 參數相符 `{d}` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-470">Everything to the right (`d`) is now matched to the route parameter `{d}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-471">下一個常值（由右至左）為 `a` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-471">The next literal, right to left, is `a`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-472">`/ab|c|d`搜尋從我們離職開始，然後 `a` 找到 `/|a|b|c|d` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-472">So `/ab|c|d` is searched starting where we left off, then `a` is found `/|a|b|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-473">右邊 () 的值 `b` 現在會符合 route 參數 `{b}` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-473">The value to the right (`b`) is now matched to the route parameter `{b}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-474">沒有剩餘的文字和剩餘的路由範本，因此這是相符的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-474">There is no remaining text and no remaining route template, so this is a match.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-475">以下是使用相同範本和 URL 路徑的負面案例範例 `/a{b}c{d}` `/aabcd` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-475">Here's an example of a negative case using the same template `/a{b}c{d}` and the URL path `/aabcd`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-476">`|`用來協助視覺化演算法的運作方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-476">The `|` is used to help visualize how the algorithm works.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-477">此案例不是相符的，這會透過相同的演算法來說明：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-477">This case isn't a match, which is explained by the same algorithm:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-478">第一個常值（由右至左）為 `c` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-478">The first literal, right to left, is `c`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-479">這 `/aabcd` 會從右側搜尋並尋找 `/aab|c|d` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-479">So `/aabcd` is searched from right and finds `/aab|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-480">右邊 () 的所有內容 `d` 現在都會與 route 參數相符 `{d}` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-480">Everything to the right (`d`) is now matched to the route parameter `{d}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-481">下一個常值（由右至左）為 `a` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-481">The next literal, right to left, is `a`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-482">`/aab|c|d`搜尋從我們離職開始，然後 `a` 找到 `/a|a|b|c|d` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-482">So `/aab|c|d` is searched starting where we left off, then `a` is found `/a|a|b|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-483">右邊 () 的值 `b` 現在會符合 route 參數 `{b}` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-483">The value to the right (`b`) is now matched to the route parameter `{b}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-484">此時有剩餘 `a` 的文字，但演算法已用完路由範本來剖析，因此這不相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-484">At this point there is remaining text `a`, but the algorithm has run out of route template to parse, so this is not a match.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-485">因為比對演算法 [是非貪婪](#greedy)的：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-485">Since the matching algorithm is [non-greedy](#greedy):</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-486">它會比對每個步驟中可能的最小文字數量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-486">It matches the smallest amount of text possible in each step.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-487">在參數值內出現分隔符號值的任何情況下，都會導致不相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-487">Any case where the delimiter value appears inside the parameter values results in not matching.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-488">正則運算式對比對行為提供更多的控制權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-488">Regular expressions provide much more control over their matching behavior.</span></span>

<a name="greedy"></a>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-489">貪婪比對（也知道 [延遲](https://wikipedia.org/wiki/Regular_expression#Lazy_matching)比對）符合最大的可能字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-489">Greedy matching, also know as [lazy matching](https://wikipedia.org/wiki/Regular_expression#Lazy_matching), matches the largest possible string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-490">非貪婪符合最小的可能字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-490">Non-greedy matches the smallest possible string.</span></span>

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-491">路由條件約束參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-491">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-492">路由條件約束執行時機是出現符合傳入 URL 的項目，並將 URL 路徑語彙基元化成路由值時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-492">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-493">路由條件約束通常會檢查透過路由範本相關聯的路由值，並針對該值是否可接受，做出 true 或 false 的決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-493">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a true or false decision about whether the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-494">某些路由條件約束會使用路由值以外的資料，以考慮是否可以路由要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-494">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-495">例如，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> 可以依據其 HTTP 指令動詞接受或拒絕要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-495">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-496">條件約束可用於路由要求和連結產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-496">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-497">請勿針對輸入驗證使用條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-497">Don't use constraints for input validation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-498">如果條件約束用於輸入驗證，則不正確輸入會導致找不到的 `404` 回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-498">If constraints are used for input validation, invalid input results in a `404` Not Found response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-499">不正確輸入應產生 `400` 錯誤的要求，並顯示適當的錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-499">Invalid input should produce a `400` Bad Request with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-500">路由條件約束會用來釐清類似的路由，而不是用來驗證特定路由的輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-500">Route constraints are used to disambiguate similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-501">下表示范範例路由條件約束及其預期行為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-501">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-502">constraint (條件約束)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-502">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-503">範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-503">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-504">範例相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-504">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-505">備註</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-505">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-506">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-506">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-507">符合任何整數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-507">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-508">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-508">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-509">符合 `true` 或 `false` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-509">Matches `true` or `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-510">不區分大小寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-510">Case-insensitive</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-511">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-511">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-512">符合非變異 `DateTime` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-512">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-513">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-513">See preceding warning.</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-514">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-514">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-515">符合非變異 `decimal` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-515">Matches a valid `decimal` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-516">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-516">See preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-517">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-517">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-518">符合非變異 `double` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-518">Matches a valid `double` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-519">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-519">See preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-520">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-520">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-521">符合非變異 `float` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-521">Matches a valid `float` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-522">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-522">See preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | `CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-523">符合有效的 `Guid` 值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-523">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-524">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-524">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-525">符合有效的 `long` 值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-525">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-526">字串必須至少有 4 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-526">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `MyFile` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-527">字串不能超過 8 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-527">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-528">字串長度必須剛好是 12 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-528">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-529">字串長度必須至少有 8 個字元，但不能超過 16 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-529">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-530">整數值必須至少為 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-530">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-531">整數值不能超過 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-531">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-532">整數值必須至少為 18，但不能超過 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-532">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-533">字串必須包含一或多個字母字元，且不區分 `a` - `z` 大小寫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-533">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters, `a`-`z` and case-insensitive.</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-534">字串必須符合正則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-534">String must match the regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-535">請參閱定義正則運算式的秘訣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-535">See tips about defining a regular expression.</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-536">用來強制執行在 URL 產生期間呈現非參數值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-536">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/regex.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-537">可以將多個冒號分隔的條件約束套用至單一參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-537">Multiple, colon delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-538">例如，下列條件約束會將參數限制在 1 或更大的整數值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-538">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-539">驗證 URL 和轉換成 CLR 類型的路由條件約束一律會使用不變的文化特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-539">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-540">例如，轉換成 CLR 類型 `int` 或 `DateTime` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-540">For example, conversion to the CLR type `int` or `DateTime`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-541">這些條件約束假設 URL 不可當地語系化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-541">These constraints assume that the URL is not localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-542">架構提供的路由條件約束不會修改路由值中儲存的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-542">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-543">所有從 URL 剖析而來的路由值會儲存為字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-543">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-544">例如，`float` 條件約束會嘗試將路由值轉換成浮點數，但轉換的值只能用來確認它可以轉換成浮點數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-544">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

### <a name="regular-expressions-in-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-545">條件約束中的正則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-545">Regular expressions in constraints</span></span>

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/regex.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-546">您可以使用路由條件約束，將正則運算式指定為內嵌條件約束 `regex(...)` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-546">Regular expressions can be specified as inline constraints using the `regex(...)` route constraint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-547">系列中的方法 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> 也接受條件約束的物件常值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-547">Methods in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> family also accept an object literal of constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-548">如果使用該表單，則會將字串值視為正則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-548">If that form is used, string values are interpreted as regular expressions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-549">下列程式碼會使用內嵌的 RegEx 條件約束：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-549">The following code uses an inline regex constraint:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/StartupRegex.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-550">下列程式碼會使用物件常值來指定 RegEx 條件約束：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-550">The following code uses an object literal to specify a regex constraint:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/StartupRegex2.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-551">ASP.NET Core 架構將 `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` 新增至規則運算式建構函式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-551">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-552">如需這些成員的說明，請參閱 <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-552">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-553">正則運算式使用的分隔符號和標記類似于路由和 c # 語言所使用的標記。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-553">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-554">規則運算式的語彙基元必須逸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-554">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-555">若要 `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` 在內嵌條件約束中使用正則運算式，請使用下列其中一項：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-555">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in an inline constraint, use one of the following:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-556">將 `\` 字串中提供的字元取代為 c # 原始檔中的字元，以將 `\\` `\` 字串 escape 字元換用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-556">Replace `\` characters provided in the string as `\\` characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-557">[逐字字串常](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-557">[Verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-558">若要將路由參數分隔符號 `{` 、 `}` 、 `[` 、 `]` ，請將運算式中的字元加倍，例如，、、 `{{` `}}` `[[` 、 `]]` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-558">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters `{`, `}`, `[`, `]`, double the characters in the expression, for example, `{{`, `}}`, `[[`, `]]`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-559">下表顯示正則運算式及其轉義版本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-559">The following table shows a regular expression and its escaped version:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-560">規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-560">Regular expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-561">已轉義的正則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-561">Escaped regular expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-562">路由中使用的正則運算式通常以 `^` 字元開頭，並符合字串的開始位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-562">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the `^` character and match the starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-563">運算式的結尾通常是 `$` 字元，並符合字串的結尾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-563">The expressions often end with the `$` character and match the end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-564">`^`和 `$` 字元可確保正則運算式符合整個路由參數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-564">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression matches the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-565">如果沒有 `^` 和 `$` 字元，正則運算式會比對字串內的任何子字串，這通常是不必要的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-565">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression matches any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-566">下表提供範例，並說明它們符合或無法符合的原因：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-566">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-567">運算是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-567">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-568">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-568">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-569">比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-569">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-570">註解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-570">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-571">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-571">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-572">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-572">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-573">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-573">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-574">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-574">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-575">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-575">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-576">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-576">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-577">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-577">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-578">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-578">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-579">符合運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-579">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-580">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-580">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-581">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-581">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-582">不區分大小寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-582">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-583">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-583">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-584">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-584">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-585">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-585">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-586">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-586">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-587">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-587">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-588">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-588">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-589">如需規則運算式語法的詳細資訊，請參閱 [.NET Framework 規則運算式](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-589">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-590">若要將參數限制為一組已知的可能值，請使用規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-590">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-591">例如，`{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` 只會將 `action` 路由值與 `list`、`get` 或 `create` 相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-591">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-592">如果已傳入條件約束字典，字串 `^(list|get|create)$` 則是對等項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-592">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-593">在條件約束字典中傳遞不符合其中一個已知條件約束的條件約束，也會被視為正則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-593">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-594">在不符合其中一個已知條件約束的範本中傳遞的條件約束，不會被視為正則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-594">Constraints that are passed  within a template that don't match one of the known constraints are not treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

### <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-595">自訂路由條件約束</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-595">Custom route constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-596">您可以藉由實作為介面來建立自訂路由條件約束 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-596">Custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-597">`IRouteConstraint`介面包含 <xref:System.Web.Routing.IRouteConstraint.Match*> ， `true` 如果滿足條件約束，則會傳回， `false` 否則會傳回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-597">The `IRouteConstraint` interface contains <xref:System.Web.Routing.IRouteConstraint.Match*>, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-598">自訂路由條件約束很少需要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-598">Custom route constraints are rarely needed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-599">在執行自訂路由條件約束之前，請考慮使用替代方法，例如模型系結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-599">Before implementing a custom route constraint, consider alternatives, such as model binding.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-600">ASP.NET Core [條件約束](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/tree/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Constraints) 資料夾提供建立條件約束的良好範例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-600">The ASP.NET Core [Constraints](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/tree/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Constraints) folder provides good examples of creating a constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-601">例如， [GuidRouteConstraint](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Constraints/GuidRouteConstraint.cs#L18)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-601">For example, [GuidRouteConstraint](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Constraints/GuidRouteConstraint.cs#L18).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-602">若要使用自訂 `IRouteConstraint` ，必須向 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 服務容器中的應用程式註冊路由條件約束類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-602">To use a custom `IRouteConstraint`, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-603">`ConstraintMap` 是一個目錄，它將路由限制式機碼對應到可驗證那些限制式的 `IRouteConstraint` 實作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-603">A `ConstraintMap` is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to `IRouteConstraint` implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-604">更新應用程式的 `ConstraintMap` 時，可在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中於進行 [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) 呼叫時更新，或透過使用 `services.Configure<RouteOptions>` 直接設定 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> 來更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-604">An app's `ConstraintMap` can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-605">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-605">For example:</span></span>

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-616">參數轉換器參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-616">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-617">參數轉換程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-617">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-618">使用產生連結時執行 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-618">Execute when generating a link using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-619">實作 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer?displayProperty=fullName>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-619">Implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer?displayProperty=fullName>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-620">是使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 進行設定的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-620">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-621">採用參數的路由值，並將它轉換為新的字串值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-621">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-622">導致在所產生連結中使用已轉換的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-622">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-623">例如，具有 `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` 之路由模式 `blog\{article:slugify}` 中的自訂 `slugify` 參數轉換器，會產生 `blog\my-test-article`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-623">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-624">請考慮下列 `IOutboundParameterTransformer` 實行：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-624">Consider the following `IOutboundParameterTransformer` implementation:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/StartupConstraint2.cs?name=snippet2)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-625">若要在路由模式中使用參數轉換，請使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 在中進行設定 `Startup.ConfigureServices` ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-625">To use a parameter transformer in a route pattern, configure it using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/StartupConstraint2.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-626">ASP.NET Core framework 會使用參數轉換器來轉換端點解析的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-626">The ASP.NET Core framework uses parameter transformers to transform the URI where an endpoint resolves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-627">例如，參數轉換器會轉換用來符合 `area` 、、和的路由 `controller` 值 `action` `page` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-627">For example, parameter transformers transform the route values used to match an `area`, `controller`, `action`, and `page`.</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapControllerRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller:slugify=Home}/{action:slugify=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-628">使用上述的路由範本，此動作 `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll` 會與 URI 相符 `/subscription-management/get-all` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-628">With the preceding route template, the action `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll` is matched with the URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-629">參數轉換器不會變更用來產生連結的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-629">A parameter transformer doesn't change the route values used to generate a link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-630">例如，`Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` 會輸出 `/subscription-management/get-all`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-630">For example, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` outputs `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-631">ASP.NET Core 提供使用參數轉換器搭配產生之路由的 API 慣例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-631">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-632"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention?displayProperty=fullName>MVC 慣例會將指定的參數轉換程式套用至應用程式中的所有屬性路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-632">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention?displayProperty=fullName> MVC convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-633">參數轉換程式會在被取代時轉換屬性路由語彙基元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-633">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-634">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用參數轉換程式自訂語彙基元取代](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-634">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-635">Razor 頁面會使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention> API 慣例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-635">Razor Pages uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention> API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-636">此慣例會將指定的參數轉換器套用至所有自動探索到的 Razor 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-636">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-637">參數轉換程式會轉換頁面路由的資料夾和檔案名區段 Razor 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-637">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-638">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用參數轉換程式自訂頁面路由](xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-638">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

<a name="ugr"></a>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-639">URL 產生參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-639">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-640">本章節包含 URL 產生所執行之演算法的參考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-640">This section contains a reference for the algorithm implemented by URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-641">在實務上，最複雜的 URL 產生範例會使用控制器或 Razor 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-641">In practice, most complex examples of URL generation use controllers or Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-642">如需其他資訊，請參閱  [控制器中的路由](xref:mvc/controllers/routing) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-642">See  [routing in controllers](xref:mvc/controllers/routing) for additional information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-643">URL 產生進程的開頭是呼叫 [LinkGenerator. GetPathByAddress](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*) 或類似的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-643">The URL generation process begins with a call to [LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*) or a similar method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-644">提供的方法有位址、一組路由值，以及有關目前要求的選擇性資訊 `HttpContext` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-644">The method is provided with an address, a set of route values, and optionally information about the current request from `HttpContext`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-645">第一個步驟是使用位址，以符合網址類別型的來解析一組候選端點 [`IEndpointAddressScheme<TAddress>`](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointAddressScheme`1) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-645">The first step is to use the address to resolve a set of candidate endpoints using an [`IEndpointAddressScheme<TAddress>`](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointAddressScheme`1) that matches the address's type.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-646">一旦位址配置找到一組候選項目之後，就會反復排序和處理端點，直到 URL 產生作業成功為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-646">Once the set of candidates is found by the address scheme, the endpoints are ordered and processed iteratively until a URL generation operation succeeds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-647">URL **產生不會檢查是否** 有多義性，傳回的第一個結果是最後的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-647">URL generation does **not** check for ambiguities, the first result returned is the final result.</span></span>

### <a name="troubleshooting-url-generation-with-logging"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-648">使用記錄針對 URL 產生進行疑難排解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-648">Troubleshooting URL generation with logging</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-649">針對 URL 產生進行疑難排解的第一個步驟，是將的記錄層級設定 `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing` 為 `TRACE` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-649">The first step in troubleshooting URL generation is setting the logging level of `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing` to `TRACE`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-650">`LinkGenerator` 記錄有關其處理的許多詳細資料，對於疑難排解問題可能很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-650">`LinkGenerator` logs many details about its processing which can be useful to troubleshoot problems.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-651">如需 URL 產生的詳細資訊，請參閱 [url 產生參考](#ugr) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-651">See [URL generation reference](#ugr) for details on URL generation.</span></span>

### <a name="addresses"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-652">位址</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-652">Addresses</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-653">位址是 URL 產生中用來將連結產生器的呼叫系結至一組候選端點的概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-653">Addresses are the concept in URL generation used to bind a call into the link generator to a set of candidate endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-654">位址是一種可延伸的概念，預設會隨附兩個執行：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-654">Addresses are an extensible concept that come with two implementations by default:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-655">使用 *端點名稱* (`string`) 作為位址：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-655">Using *endpoint name* (`string`) as the address:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-656">提供類似于 MVC 之路由名稱的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-656">Provides similar functionality to MVC's route name.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-657">使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointNameMetadata> 元資料類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-657">Uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointNameMetadata> metadata type.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-658">針對所有已註冊端點的中繼資料解析提供的字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-658">Resolves the provided string against the metadata of all registered endpoints.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-659">如果多個端點使用相同的名稱，則會在啟動時擲回例外狀況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-659">Throws an exception on startup if multiple endpoints use the same name.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-660">建議用於在控制器和頁面之外使用一般用途 Razor 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-660">Recommended for general-purpose use outside of controllers and Razor Pages.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-661">使用 *路由值* (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteValuesAddress>) 作為位址：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-661">Using *route values* (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteValuesAddress>) as the address:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-662">提供類似于控制器和 Razor 頁面舊版 URL 產生的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-662">Provides similar functionality to controllers and Razor Pages legacy URL generation.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-663">非常複雜，可進行擴充和調試。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-663">Very complex to extend and debug.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-664">提供所使用的實作為、標籤協助程式 `IUrlHelper` 、HTML 協助程式、動作結果等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-664">Provides the implementation used by `IUrlHelper`, Tag Helpers, HTML Helpers, Action Results, etc.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-665">位址配置的角色是將位址和相符端點之間的關聯設為任意準則：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-665">The role of the address scheme is to make the association between the address and matching endpoints by arbitrary criteria:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-666">端點名稱配置會執行基本的字典查閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-666">The endpoint name scheme performs a basic dictionary lookup.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-667">路由值配置具有複雜的集合演算法的最佳子集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-667">The route values scheme has a complex best subset of set algorithm.</span></span>

<a name="ambient"></a>

### <a name="ambient-values-and-explicit-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-668">環境值和明確值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-668">Ambient values and explicit values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-669">從目前的要求中，路由會存取目前要求的路由值 `HttpContext.Request.RouteValues` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-669">From the current request, routing accesses the route values of the current request `HttpContext.Request.RouteValues`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-670">與目前要求相關聯的值稱為 **環境值**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-670">The values associated with the current request are referred to as the **ambient values**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-671">為了清楚起見，檔是指將傳入方法的路由值視為 **明確值**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-671">For the purpose of clarity, the documentation refers to the route values passed in to methods as **explicit values**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-672">下列範例會顯示環境值和明確值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-672">The following example shows ambient values and explicit values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-673">它會從目前的要求和明確的值提供環境 `{ id = 17, }` 值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-673">It provides ambient values from the current request and explicit values: `{ id = 17, }`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-675">傳回 `/Widget/Index/17`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-675">Returns `/Widget/Index/17`</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-682">`/Gadget/Edit/17` 傳回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-682">`/Gadget/Edit/17` is returned.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-683"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ControllerBase.Url> 取得 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-683"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ControllerBase.Url> gets the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Action*>   
<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-684">使用動作方法的絕對路徑產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-684">generates a URL with an absolute path for an action method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-685">URL 包含指定的 `action` 名稱和 `route` 值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-685">The URL contains the specified `action` name and `route` values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-686">下列程式碼會從目前的要求和明確的值提供環境 `{ page = "./Edit, id = 17, }` 值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-686">The following code provides ambient values from the current request and explicit values: `{ page = "./Edit, id = 17, }`:</span></span>
