<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-687">`url` `/Edit/17` 當 [編輯] Razor 頁面包含下列頁面指示詞時，上述程式碼會設定為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-687">The preceding code sets `url` to  `/Edit/17` when the Edit Razor Page contains the following page directive:</span></span>

 `@page "{id:int}"`

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-688">如果編輯頁面未包含 `"{id:int}"` 路由範本， `url` 則為 `/Edit?id=17` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-688">If the Edit page doesn't contain the `"{id:int}"` route template, `url` is `/Edit?id=17`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-689"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>除了此處所述的規則之外，MVC 的行為還會增加一層複雜性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-689">The behavior of MVC's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> adds a layer of complexity in addition to the rules described here:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-690">`IUrlHelper` 一律提供來自目前要求的路由值做為環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-690">`IUrlHelper` always provides the route values from the current request as ambient values.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-691">除非由開發人員覆寫，否則[IUrlHelper](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Action*)一律會將目前的 `action` 和 `controller` 路由值複製為明確值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-691">[IUrlHelper.Action](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Action*) always copies the current `action` and `controller` route values as explicit values unless overridden by the developer.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-692">除非覆寫，否則[IUrlHelper](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*)一律會將目前的 `page` 路由值複製為明確值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-692">[IUrlHelper.Page](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*) always copies the current `page` route value as an explicit value unless overridden.</span></span> <!--by the user-->
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-693">`IUrlHelper.Page` 除非覆寫，否則一律以明確值覆寫目前的 `handler` 路由值 `null` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-693">`IUrlHelper.Page` always overrides the current `handler` route value with `null` as an explicit values unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-694">使用者通常會因為環境值的行為詳細資料而感到驚訝，因為 MVC 似乎不會遵循自己的規則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-694">Users are often surprised by the behavioral details of ambient values, because MVC doesn't seem to follow its own rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-695">基於歷程記錄和相容性的理由，某些路由值（例如 `action` 、 `controller` 、 `page` 和） `handler` 有自己的特殊案例行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-695">For historical and compatibility reasons, certain route values such as `action`, `controller`, `page`, and `handler` have their own special-case behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-696">提供的對等功能 `LinkGenerator.GetPathByAction` 會 `LinkGenerator.GetPathByPage` `IUrlHelper` 針對相容性複製這些異常。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-696">The equivalent functionality provided by `LinkGenerator.GetPathByAction` and `LinkGenerator.GetPathByPage` duplicates these anomalies of `IUrlHelper` for compatibility.</span></span>

### <a name="url-generation-process"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-697">URL 產生進程</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-697">URL generation process</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-698">一旦找到候選端點集合之後，URL 產生演算法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-698">Once the set of candidate endpoints are found, the URL generation algorithm:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-699">反復處理端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-699">Processes the endpoints iteratively.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-700">傳回第一個成功的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-700">Returns the first successful result.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-701">此程式中的第一個步驟是呼叫 **路由值失效**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-701">The first step in this process is called **route value invalidation**.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-702">路由值失效是路由用來決定應該使用環境值的路由值，以及應忽略哪些路由值的處理常式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-702">Route value invalidation is the process by which routing decides which route values from the ambient values should be used and which should be ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-703">會考慮每個環境的值，並結合明確的值，或忽略此值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-703">Each ambient value is considered and either combined with the explicit values, or ignored.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-704">考慮環境值角色的最佳方式，就是在某些常見的情況下，他們會嘗試儲存應用程式開發人員的輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-704">The best way to think about the role of ambient values is that they attempt to save application developers typing, in some common cases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-705">傳統上，環境值很有説明的情況與 MVC 相關：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-705">Traditionally, the scenarios where ambient values are helpful are related to MVC:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-706">連結至相同控制器中的另一個動作時，不需要指定控制器名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-706">When linking to another action in the same controller, the controller name doesn't need to be specified.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-707">連結到相同區域中的另一個控制器時，不需要指定區功能變數名稱稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-707">When linking to another controller in the same area, the area name doesn't need to be specified.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-708">連結至相同的動作方法時，不需要指定路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-708">When linking to the same action method, route values don't need to be specified.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-709">連結到應用程式的另一個部分時，您不會想要在應用程式的該部分中執行沒有意義的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-709">When linking to another part of the app, you don't want to carry over route values that have no meaning in that part of the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-710">呼叫或傳回傳回 `LinkGenerator` `IUrlHelper` 的 `null` 原因通常是因為不了解路由值失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-710">Calls to `LinkGenerator` or `IUrlHelper` that return `null` are usually caused by not understanding route value invalidation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-711">明確指定更多路由值以查看是否能解決問題，以針對路由值失效進行疑難排解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-711">Troubleshoot route value invalidation by explicitly specifying more of the route values to see if that solves the problem.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-712">路由值失效的運作方式是假設應用程式的 URL 配置為階層式，且階層是由左至右形成的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-712">Route value invalidation works on the assumption that the app's URL scheme is hierarchical, with a hierarchy formed from left-to-right.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-713">請考慮使用基本控制器路由範本 `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` ，以直覺瞭解這在實務上的運作方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-713">Consider the basic controller route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` to get an intuitive sense of how this works in practice.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-714">值的 **變更** 會使出現在右邊的所有路由值 **失效** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-714">A **change** to a value **invalidates** all of the route values that appear to the right.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-715">這會反映階層的假設。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-715">This reflects the assumption about hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-716">如果應用程式具有的環境值 `id` ，且此作業為指定了不同的值 `controller` ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-716">If the app has an ambient value for `id`, and the operation specifies a different value for the `controller`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-717">`id` 因為是左邊的，所以不會重複使用 `{controller}` `{id?}` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-717">`id` won't be reused because `{controller}` is to the left of `{id?}`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-718">示範此原則的一些範例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-718">Some examples demonstrating this principle:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-719">如果明確的值包含的值 `id` ，的環境值會被 `id` 忽略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-719">If the explicit values contain a value for `id`, the ambient value for `id` is ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-720">您 `controller` 可以使用和的環境值 `action` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-720">The ambient values for `controller` and `action` can be used.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-721">如果明確的值包含的值 `action` ，的任何環境值 `action` 都會被忽略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-721">If the explicit values contain a value for `action`, any ambient value for `action` is ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-722">您可以使用的環境值 `controller` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-722">The ambient values for `controller` can be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-723">如果的明確值與 `action` 的環境值不同 `action` ，將 `id` 不會使用此值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-723">If the explicit value for `action` is different from the ambient value for `action`, the `id` value won't be used.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-724">如果的明確值與 `action` 的環境值相同 `action` ，則 `id` 可以使用此值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-724">If the explicit value for `action` is the same as the ambient value for `action`, the `id` value can be used.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-725">如果明確的值包含的值 `controller` ，的任何環境值 `controller` 都會被忽略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-725">If the explicit values contain a value for `controller`, any ambient value for `controller` is ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-726">如果的明確值與 `controller` 的環境值不同 `controller` ，將 `action` 不會使用和 `id` 值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-726">If the explicit value for `controller` is different from the ambient value for `controller`, the `action` and `id` values won't be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-727">如果的明確值與 `controller` 的環境值相同 `controller` ，則 `action` `id` 可以使用和值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-727">If the explicit value for `controller` is the same as the ambient value for `controller`, the `action` and `id` values can be used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-728">此程式會因為屬性路由和專用慣例路由的存在而變得更複雜。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-728">This process is further complicated by the existence of attribute routes and dedicated conventional routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-729">控制器慣例路由，例如 `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` 使用路由參數指定階層。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-729">Controller conventional routes such as `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` specify a hierarchy using route parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-730">適用于控制器和頁面的 [專用傳統路由](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#dcr) 和 [屬性路由](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#ar) Razor ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-730">For [dedicated conventional routes](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#dcr) and [attribute routes](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#ar) to controllers and Razor Pages:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-731">有路由值的階層。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-731">There is a hierarchy of route values.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-732">它們不會出現在範本中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-732">They don't appear in the template.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-733">在這些情況下，URL 產生會定義 **必要的值** 概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-733">For these cases, URL generation defines the **required values** concept.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-734">控制器和頁面所建立的端點 Razor 都具有指定的值，可讓路由值失效運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-734">Endpoints created by controllers and Razor Pages have required values specified that allow route value invalidation to work.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-735">路由值失效演算法的詳細資料：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-735">The route value invalidation algorithm in detail:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-736">必要的值名稱會與路由參數合併，然後由左至右處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-736">The required value names are combined with the route parameters, then processed from left-to-right.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-737">針對每個參數，會比較環境值和明確值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-737">For each parameter, the ambient value and explicit value are compared:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-738">如果環境值和明確值相同，進程會繼續執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-738">If the ambient value and explicit value are the same, the process continues.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-739">如果環境值存在且明確值不是，則會在產生 URL 時使用環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-739">If the ambient value is present and the explicit value isn't, the ambient value is used when generating the URL.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-740">如果環境值不存在且明確的值為，則會拒絕環境值和所有後續的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-740">If the ambient value isn't present and the explicit value is, reject the ambient value and all subsequent ambient values.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-741">如果有環境值和明確的值，而且這兩個值不同，則會拒絕環境值和所有後續的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-741">If the ambient value and the explicit value are present, and the two values are different, reject the ambient value and all subsequent ambient values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-742">此時，URL 產生作業已準備好評估路由條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-742">At this point, the URL generation operation is ready to evaluate route constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-743">接受的值集合會與提供給條件約束的參數預設值結合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-743">The set of accepted values is combined with the parameter default values, which is provided to constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-744">如果所有條件約束都通過，則作業會繼續進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-744">If the constraints all pass, the operation continues.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-745">接下來，可以使用 **接受的值** 來展開路由範本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-745">Next, the **accepted values** can be used to expand the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-746">路由範本的處理：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-746">The route template is processed:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-747">從左至右。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-747">From left-to-right.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-748">每個參數都有接受的值取代。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-748">Each parameter has its accepted value substituted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-749">使用下列特殊案例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-749">With the following special cases:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-750">如果接受的值遺漏值，而且參數有預設值，則會使用預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-750">If the accepted values is missing a value and the parameter has a default value, the default value is used.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-751">如果接受的值遺漏值，而且參數是選擇性的，則會繼續處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-751">If the accepted values is missing a value and the parameter is optional, processing continues.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-752">如果遺漏選擇性參數右邊的任何路由參數都有值，則作業會失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-752">If any route parameter to the right of a missing optional parameter has a value, the operation fails.</span></span>
  * <!-- review default-valued parameters optional parameters --> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-753">可能的話，會折迭連續的預設值參數和選擇性參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-753">Contiguous default-valued parameters and optional parameters are collapsed where possible.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-754">明確提供但不符合路由區段的值會新增至查詢字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-754">Values explicitly provided that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-755">下表顯示使用路由範本 `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` 時的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-755">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-756">環境值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-756">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-757">明確值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-757">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-758">結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-758">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-759">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-759">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-760">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-760">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-761">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-761">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-762">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-762">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-763">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-763">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-764">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-764">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-765">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-765">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-766">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-766">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

### <a name="problems-with-route-value-invalidation"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-767">路由值失效的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-767">Problems with route value invalidation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-768">從 ASP.NET Core 3.0 開始，舊版 ASP.NET Core 中使用的某些 URL 產生配置，不適用於 URL 產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-768">As of ASP.NET Core 3.0, some URL generation schemes used in earlier ASP.NET Core versions don't work well with URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-769">ASP.NET Core 小組計畫在未來的版本中新增功能來解決這些需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-769">The ASP.NET Core team plans to add features to address these needs in a future release.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-770">現在，最好的解決方法是使用舊版路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-770">For now the best solution is to use legacy routing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-771">下列程式碼顯示路由不支援的 URL 產生配置範例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-771">The following code shows an example of a URL generation scheme that's not supported by routing.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/StartupUnsupported.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-772">在上述程式碼中， `culture` 會使用 route 參數進行當地語系化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-772">In the preceding code, the `culture` route parameter is used for localization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-773">希望將 `culture` 參數一律接受為環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-773">The desire is to have the `culture` parameter always accepted as an ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-774">不過， `culture` 因為所需的值運作方式，所以不接受參數作為環境值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-774">However, the `culture` parameter is not accepted as an ambient value because of the way required values work:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-775">在 `"default"` 路由範本中， `culture` 路由參數是左邊的 `controller` ，因此的變更將 `controller` 不會失效 `culture` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-775">In the `"default"` route template, the `culture` route parameter is to the left of `controller`, so changes to `controller` won't invalidate `culture`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-776">在 `"blog"` 路由範本中， `culture` 路由參數會被視為 `controller` 出現在必要值中的右邊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-776">In the `"blog"` route template, the `culture` route parameter is considered to be to the right of `controller`, which appears in the required values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-778">下列連結提供設定端點中繼資料的相關資訊：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-778">The following links provide information on configuring endpoint metadata:</span></span>

<a name="hostmatch"></a>

## <a name="host-matching-in-routes-with-requirehost"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-784">使用 RequireHost 的路由中的主機相符</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-784">Host matching in routes with RequireHost</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-785"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireHost*> 將條件約束套用至需要指定主機的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-785"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireHost*> applies a constraint to the route which requires the specified host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-786">`RequireHost`或[[Host]](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.HostAttribute)參數可以是：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-786">The `RequireHost` or [[Host]](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.HostAttribute) parameter can be:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-787">Host： `www.domain.com` ，符合 `www.domain.com` 任何埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-787">Host: `www.domain.com`, matches `www.domain.com` with any port.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-788">具有萬用字元的主機： `*.domain.com` 、 `www.domain.com` 比 `subdomain.domain.com` 對、或 `www.subdomain.domain.com` 在任何埠上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-788">Host with wildcard: `*.domain.com`, matches `www.domain.com`, `subdomain.domain.com`, or `www.subdomain.domain.com` on any port.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-789">埠：與 `*:5000` 任何主機相符的埠5000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-789">Port: `*:5000`, matches port 5000 with any host.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-790">主機和埠： `www.domain.com:5000` 或 `*.domain.com:5000` 符合主機和埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-790">Host and port: `www.domain.com:5000` or `*.domain.com:5000`, matches host and port.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-791">您可以使用或來指定多個參數 `RequireHost` `[Host]` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-791">Multiple parameters can be specified using `RequireHost` or `[Host]`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-792">條件約束符合任何參數的有效主機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-792">The constraint  matches hosts valid for any of the parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-793">例如， `[Host("domain.com", "*.domain.com")]` 符合 `domain.com` 、 `www.domain.com` 和 `subdomain.domain.com` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-793">For example, `[Host("domain.com", "*.domain.com")]` matches `domain.com`, `www.domain.com`, and `subdomain.domain.com`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-794">下列程式碼會使用 `RequireHost` 來要求路由上指定的主機：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-794">The following code uses `RequireHost` to require the specified host on the route:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/StartupRequireHost.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-795">下列程式碼會使用 `[Host]` 控制器上的屬性來要求任何指定的主機：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-795">The following code uses the `[Host]` attribute on the controller to require any of the specified hosts:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-796">當 `[Host]` 屬性同時套用至控制器和動作方法時：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-796">When the `[Host]` attribute is applied to both the controller and action method:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-798">控制器屬性會被忽略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-798">The controller attribute is ignored.</span></span>

## <a name="performance-guidance-for-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-799">路由的效能指引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-799">Performance guidance for routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-800">大部分的路由會在 ASP.NET Core 3.0 中更新，以提升效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-800">Most of routing was updated in ASP.NET Core 3.0 to increase performance.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-801">當應用程式發生效能問題時，通常會將路由視為問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-801">When an app has performance problems, routing is often suspected as the problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-802">考慮路由的原因是，控制器和 Razor 頁面等架構會報告在架構中的記錄訊息內花費的時間量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-802">The reason routing is suspected is that frameworks like controllers and Razor Pages report the amount of time spent inside the framework in their logging messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-803">當控制器所報告的時間與要求的總時間之間有顯著的差異時：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-803">When there's a significant difference between the time reported by controllers and the total time of the request:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-804">開發人員會將其應用程式程式碼消除為問題的根源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-804">Developers eliminate their app code as the source of the problem.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-805">通常會假設路由是原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-805">It's common to assume routing is the cause.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-806">路由是使用上千個端點測試的效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-806">Routing is performance tested using thousands of endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-807">一般的應用程式不太可能只會因為太大而遇到效能問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-807">It's unlikely that a typical app will encounter a performance problem just by being too large.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-808">緩慢路由效能最常見的根本原因，通常是行為錯誤的自訂中介軟體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-808">The most common root cause of slow routing performance is usually a badly-behaving custom middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-809">下列程式碼範例示範縮小延遲來源的基本技術：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-809">This following code sample demonstrates a basic technique for narrowing down the source of delay:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/StartupDelay.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-810">到時間路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-810">To time routing:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-811">將每個中介軟體與先前程式碼中顯示的計時中介軟體複本交錯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-811">Interleave each middleware with a copy of the timing middleware shown in the preceding code.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-812">加入唯一識別碼，將計時資料與程式碼產生關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-812">Add a unique identifier to correlate the timing data with the code.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-813">這是在很重要的情況下縮小延遲的基本方法，例如，超過 `10ms` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-813">This is a basic way to narrow down the delay when it's significant, for example, more than `10ms`.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-814">減去 `Time 2` `Time 1` 中介軟體內花費的時間 `UseRouting` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-814">Subtracting `Time 2` from `Time 1` reports the time spent inside the `UseRouting` middleware.</span></span>

### <a name="potentially-expensive-routing-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-816">可能昂貴的路由功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-816">Potentially expensive routing features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-817">下列清單提供對路由功能的一些深入解析，相較于基本路由範本，這些功能相當昂貴：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-817">The following list provides some insight into routing features that are relatively expensive compared with basic route templates:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-818">正則運算式：可以撰寫很複雜的正則運算式，或具有少量輸入的長時間執行時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-818">Regular expressions: It's possible to write regular expressions that are complex, or have long running time with a small amount of input.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-819"> () 的複雜區段 `{x}-{y}-{z}` ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-819">Complex segments (`{x}-{y}-{z}`):</span></span> 
  * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-820">比剖析一般 URL 路徑區段更昂貴。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-820">Are significantly more expensive than parsing a regular URL path segment.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-821">會產生更多的子字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-821">Result in many more substrings being allocated.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-822">ASP.NET Core 3.0 路由效能更新中未更新複雜區段邏輯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-822">The complex segment logic was not updated in ASP.NET Core 3.0 routing performance update.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-823">同步資料存取：許多複雜的應用程式在其路由中都有資料庫存取權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-823">Synchronous data access: Many complex apps have database access as part of their routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-824">ASP.NET Core 2.2 和較早的路由可能無法提供支援資料庫存取路由的適當擴充性點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-824">ASP.NET Core 2.2 and earlier routing might not provide the right extensibility points to support database access routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-825">例如， <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 和 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ActionConstraints.IActionConstraint> 是同步的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-825">For example, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ActionConstraints.IActionConstraint> are synchronous.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-826">和等擴充點 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy> <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointSelectorContext> 都是非同步。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-826">Extensibility points such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointSelectorContext> are asynchronous.</span></span>

## <a name="guidance-for-library-authors"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-827">程式庫作者指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-827">Guidance for library authors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-828">本節包含程式庫作者在路由上建立的指引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-828">This section contains guidance for library authors building on top of routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-829">這些詳細資料的目的是要確保應用程式開發人員使用延伸路由的程式庫和架構有良好的體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-829">These details are intended to ensure that app developers have a good experience using libraries and frameworks that extend routing.</span></span>

### <a name="define-endpoints"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-830">定義端點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-830">Define endpoints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-831">若要建立使用路由進行 URL 比對的架構，請先定義以之上建立的使用者體驗 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-831">To create a framework that uses routing for URL matching, start by defining a user experience that builds on top of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-832">在之上 **進行** build <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-832">**DO** build on top of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-833">這可讓使用者使用其他 ASP.NET Core 功能來撰寫您的架構，而不會造成混淆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-833">This allows users to compose your framework with other ASP.NET Core features without confusion.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-834">每個 ASP.NET Core 範本都包含路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-834">Every ASP.NET Core template includes routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-835">假設路由存在且熟悉使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-835">Assume routing is present and familiar for users.</span></span>

```csharp
app.UseEndpoints(endpoints =>
{
    // Your framework
    endpoints.MapMyFramework(...);

    endpoints.MapHealthChecks("/healthz");
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-836">**確實** 從呼叫傳回密封的具象型別 `MapMyFramework(...)` <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IEndpointConventionBuilder> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-836">**DO** return a sealed concrete type from a call to `MapMyFramework(...)` that implements <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IEndpointConventionBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-837">大部分 `Map...` 的 framework 方法都遵循此模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-837">Most framework `Map...` methods follow this pattern.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-838">`IEndpointConventionBuilder`介面：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-838">The `IEndpointConventionBuilder` interface:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-839">允許中繼資料的可組合性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-839">Allows composability of metadata.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-840">的目標是各種擴充方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-840">Is targeted by a variety of extension methods.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-841">宣告您自己的型別可讓您將自己的架構專屬功能新增至建立器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-841">Declaring your own type allows you to add your own framework-specific functionality to the builder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-842">您可以包裝架構宣告的產生器，並將呼叫轉寄給它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-842">It's ok to wrap a framework-declared builder and forward calls to it.</span></span>

```csharp
app.UseEndpoints(endpoints =>
{
    // Your framework
    endpoints.MapMyFramework(...).RequireAuthorization()
                                 .WithMyFrameworkFeature(awesome: true);

    endpoints.MapHealthChecks("/healthz");
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-843">**請考慮** 撰寫您自己 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> 的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-843">**CONSIDER** writing your own <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-844">`EndpointDataSource` 這是用來宣告和更新端點集合的低層級基本類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-844">`EndpointDataSource` is the low-level primitive for declaring and updating a collection of endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-845">`EndpointDataSource` 是控制器和頁面所使用的強大 API Razor 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-845">`EndpointDataSource` is a powerful API used by controllers and Razor Pages.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-846">路由測試有一個基本的不可更新資料來源 [範例](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/test/testassets/RoutingSandbox/Framework/FrameworkEndpointDataSource.cs#L17) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-846">The routing tests have a [basic example](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/test/testassets/RoutingSandbox/Framework/FrameworkEndpointDataSource.cs#L17) of a non-updating data source.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-847">預設 **不** 嘗試註冊 `EndpointDataSource` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-847">**DO NOT** attempt to register an `EndpointDataSource` by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-848">要求使用者在中註冊您的架構 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-848">Require users to register your framework in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-849">路由的原理是，預設不會包含任何專案，而且這 `UseEndpoints` 是註冊端點的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-849">The philosophy of routing is that nothing is included by default, and that `UseEndpoints` is the place to register endpoints.</span></span>

### <a name="creating-routing-integrated-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-850">建立路由整合中介軟體</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-850">Creating routing-integrated middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-851">**請考慮** 將元資料類型定義為介面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-851">**CONSIDER** defining metadata types as an interface.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-852">**請盡可能** 使用元資料類型做為類別和方法上的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-852">**DO** make it possible to use metadata types as an attribute on classes and methods.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/ICoolMetadata.cs?name=snippet2)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-853">控制器和頁面等架構 Razor 支援將中繼資料屬性套用至類型和方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-853">Frameworks like controllers and Razor Pages support applying metadata attributes to types and methods.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-854">如果您宣告元資料類型：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-854">If you declare metadata types:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-855">讓它們可作為 [屬性](/dotnet/csharp/programming-guide/concepts/attributes/)存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-855">Make them accessible as [attributes](/dotnet/csharp/programming-guide/concepts/attributes/).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-856">大部分的使用者都很熟悉套用屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-856">Most users are familiar with applying attributes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-857">將元資料類型宣告為介面，可增加另一層彈性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-857">Declaring a metadata type as an interface adds another layer of flexibility:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-858">介面是可組合的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-858">Interfaces are composable.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-859">開發人員可以宣告自己的類型，以結合多個原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-859">Developers can declare their own types that combine multiple policies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-860">**請確定可以** 覆寫中繼資料，如下列範例所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-860">**DO** make it possible to override metadata, as shown in the following example:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/ICoolMetadata.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-861">遵循這些指導方針的最佳方式是避免定義 **標記中繼資料**：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-861">The best way to follow these guidelines is to avoid defining **marker metadata**:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-862">請不要只尋找元資料類型是否存在。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-862">Don't just look for the presence of a metadata type.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-863">在中繼資料上定義屬性，並檢查屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-863">Define a property on the metadata and check the property.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-864">元資料集合已排序，並支援依優先順序覆寫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-864">The metadata collection is ordered and supports overriding by priority.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-865">在控制器的案例中，動作方法上的中繼資料最特定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-865">In the case of controllers, metadata on the action method is most specific.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-866">**讓中間** 件在使用和沒有路由的情況下很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-866">**DO** make middleware useful with and without routing.</span></span>

```csharp
app.UseRouting();

app.UseAuthorization(new AuthorizationPolicy() { ... });

app.UseEndpoints(endpoints =>
{
    // Your framework
    endpoints.MapMyFramework(...).RequireAuthorization();
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-867">作為此指導方針的範例，請考慮使用 `UseAuthorization` 中介軟體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-867">As an example of this guideline, consider the `UseAuthorization` middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-868">授權中介軟體可讓您傳入回原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-868">The authorization middleware allows you to pass in a fallback policy.</span></span> <!-- shown where?  (shown here) --> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-869">若有指定，則會同時套用至這兩個原則：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-869">The fallback policy, if specified, applies to both:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-870">沒有指定原則的端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-870">Endpoints without a specified policy.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-871">不符合端點的要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-871">Requests that don't match an endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-872">這使得授權中介軟體在路由的內容之外很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-872">This makes the authorization middleware useful outside of the context of routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-873">授權中介軟體可用於傳統中介軟體程式設計。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-873">The authorization middleware can be used for traditional middleware programming.</span></span>

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/dbg-route.md)]

::: moniker-end

::: moniker range="= aspnetcore-2.2"

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-874">路由負責將要求 Uri 對應至端點，並將傳入要求分派至這些端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-874">Routing is responsible for mapping request URIs to endpoints and dispatching incoming requests to those endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-875">路由定義於應用程式，並在該應用程式啟動時進行設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-875">Routes are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-876">路由可以選擇性地從要求中所包含的 URL 擷取值，然後這些值就可用於處理要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-876">A route can optionally extract values from the URL contained in the request, and these values can then be used for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-877">使用應用程式中的路由資訊，路由也能夠產生對應至端點的 Url。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-877">Using route information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-878">若要使用 ASP.NET Core 2.2 中的最新路由情節，請將[相容性版本](xref:mvc/compatibility-version)指定為 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中的 MVC 服務註冊：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-878">To use the latest routing scenarios in ASP.NET Core 2.2, specify the [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) to the MVC services registration in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddMvc()
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_2);
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-879"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.MvcOptions.EnableEndpointRouting> 選項會決定路由功能應該在內部使用以端點為基礎的邏輯，或以 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 為基礎的邏輯 (適用於 ASP.NET Core 2.1 或更舊版本)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-879">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.MvcOptions.EnableEndpointRouting> option determines if routing should internally use endpoint-based logic or the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based logic of ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-880">當相容性版本設定為 2.2 或更新版本時，預設值為 `true`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-880">When the compatibility version is set to 2.2 or later, the default value is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-881">將值設定為 `false` 可使用舊版路由邏輯：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-881">Set the value to `false` to use the prior routing logic:</span></span>

```csharp
// Use the routing logic of ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier:
services.AddMvc(options => options.EnableEndpointRouting = false)
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_2);
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-882">如需以 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 為基礎之路由的詳細資訊，請參閱[本主題的 ASP.NET Core 2.1 版本](?view=aspnetcore-2.1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-882">For more information on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, see the [ASP.NET Core 2.1 version of this topic](?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-883">本文件涵蓋低階的 ASP.NET Core 路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-883">This document covers low-level ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-884">如需 ASP.NET Core MVC 路由的資訊，請參閱 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-884">For information on ASP.NET Core MVC routing, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-885">如需頁面中路由慣例的詳細資訊 Razor ，請參閱 <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-885">For information on routing conventions in Razor Pages, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-886">[查看或下載範例程式碼](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([如何下載](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-886">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-887">路由的基本概念</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-887">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-888">大部分應用程式都應該選擇基本的描述性路由傳送配置，讓 URL 可讀且有意義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-888">Most apps should choose a basic and descriptive routing scheme so that URLs are readable and meaningful.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-889">預設慣例路由 `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-889">The default conventional route `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-890">支援基本的描述性路由配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-890">Supports a basic and descriptive routing scheme.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-891">適合作為 UI 型應用程式的起點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-891">Is a useful starting point for UI-based apps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-892">開發人員通常會在使用 [屬性路由](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) 或專用慣例路由的特殊情況下，將額外的簡易路由新增到應用程式的高流量區域中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-892">Developers commonly add additional terse routes to high-traffic areas of an app in specialized situations using [attribute routing](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) or dedicated conventional routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-893">特殊化的情況範例包括、blog 和電子商務端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-893">Specialized situations examples include, blog and ecommerce endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-894">Web API 應該使用屬性路由傳送來將應用程式功能模型建構為作業由 HTTP 指令動詞代表的資源集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-894">Web APIs should use attribute routing to model the app's functionality as a set of resources where operations are represented by HTTP verbs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-895">這表示相同邏輯資源上的許多作業（例如 GET 和 POST）都會使用相同的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-895">This means that many operations, for example, GET, and POST, on the same logical resource use the same URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-896">屬性路由提供仔細設計 API 公用端點配置所需的控制層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-896">Attribute routing provides a level of control that's needed to carefully design an API's public endpoint layout.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-897">Razor 頁面應用程式會使用預設的傳統路由，在應用程式的 *Pages* 資料夾中提供命名資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-897">Razor Pages apps use default conventional routing to serve named resources in the *Pages* folder of an app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-898">有其他慣例可讓您自訂 Razor 頁面路由行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-898">Additional conventions are available that allow you to customize Razor Pages routing behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-899">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 <xref:razor-pages/index> 和 <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-899">For more information, see <xref:razor-pages/index> and <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-900">URL 產生支援允許在不需要硬式編碼的 URL 來連結應用程式的情況下開發應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-900">URL generation support allows the app to be developed without hard-coding URLs to link the app together.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-901">這項支援可讓您從基本路由設定開始，並在決定應用程式資源配置之後修改路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-901">This support allows for starting with a basic routing configuration and modifying the routes after the app's resource layout is determined.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-902">路由會使用 *端點* (`Endpoint`) 來代表應用程式中的邏輯端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-902">Routing uses *endpoints* (`Endpoint`) to represent logical endpoints in an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-903">端點會定義用來處理要求的一項委派及一個任意中繼資料集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-903">An endpoint defines a delegate to process requests and a collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-904">中繼資料可根據附加至每個端點的原則和組態，來實作跨領域關注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-904">The metadata is used implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-905">路由系統具有下列特性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-905">The routing system has the following characteristics:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-906">使用路由範本語法以 Token 化路由參數來定義路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-906">Route template syntax is used to define routes with tokenized route parameters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-907">允許傳統式和屬性式端點組態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-907">Conventional-style and attribute-style endpoint configuration is permitted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-908"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 可用來判斷 URL 參數是否包含對指定端點條件約束有效的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-908"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> is used to determine whether a URL parameter contains a valid value for a given endpoint constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-909">應用程式模型（例如 MVC/ Razor Pages）會註冊其所有端點，這些端點具有可預測的路由案例執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-909">App models, such as MVC/Razor Pages, register all of their endpoints, which have a predictable implementation of routing scenarios.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-910">路由實作會在中介軟體管線需要時制定路由決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-910">The routing implementation makes routing decisions wherever desired in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-911">在路由中介軟體之後出現的中介軟體可以檢查指定要求 URI 的路由中介軟體端點決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-911">Middleware that appears after a Routing Middleware can inspect the result of the Routing Middleware's endpoint decision for a given request URI.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-912">您可以針對中介軟體管線中任何位置的應用程式，列舉其中的所有端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-912">It's possible to enumerate all of the endpoints in the app anywhere in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-913">應用程式可以根據端點資訊使用路由來產生 URL (例如，針對重新導向或連結)，因此避免硬式編碼的 URL，這有助於可維護性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-913">An app can use routing to generate URLs (for example, for redirection or links) based on endpoint information and thus avoid hard-coded URLs, which helps maintainability.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-914">URL 是根據支援任意擴充性的位址所產生：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-914">URL generation is based on addresses, which support arbitrary extensibility:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-915">您可以在任何位置使用[相依性插入 (DI)](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection) 來解析連結產生器 API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>)，以產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-915">The Link Generator API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>) can be resolved anywhere using [dependency injection (DI)](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection) to generate URLs.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-916">如果無法透過 DI 使用連結產生器 API，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 會提供方法來建立 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-916">Where the Link Generator API isn't available via DI, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> offers methods to build URLs.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-917">當 ASP.NET Core 2.2 中的端點路由發行時，端點連結僅限於 MVC/ Razor 頁面動作和頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-917">With the release of endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2, endpoint linking is limited to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-918">未來版本將規劃擴充端點連結功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-918">The expansions of endpoint-linking capabilities is planned for future releases.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-919">路由會透過 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> 類別連線到[中介軟體](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index)管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-919">Routing is connected to the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-920">[ASP.NET CORE mvc](xref:mvc/overview) 會將路由新增至中介軟體管線，作為其設定的一部分，並處理 MVC 和 Razor 頁面應用程式中的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-920">[ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) adds routing to the middleware pipeline as part of its configuration and handles routing in MVC and Razor Pages apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-921">若要了解如何使用路由作為獨立元件，請參閱[使用路由中介軟體](#use-routing-middleware)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-921">To learn how to use routing as a standalone component, see the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section.</span></span>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-922">URL 比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-922">URL matching</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-923">URL 比對是路由用來將傳入要求分派給「端點」的處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-923">URL matching is the process by which routing dispatches an incoming request to an *endpoint*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-924">這個處理序是基於 URL 路徑中的資料，但是可以擴展為考慮要求中的任何資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-924">This process is based on data in the URL path but can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-925">分派要求給不同處理常式的能力，是調整應用程式大小和複雜度的關鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-925">The ability to dispatch requests to separate handlers is key to scaling the size and complexity of an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-926">端點路由中的路由系統負責制定所有分派決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-926">The routing system in endpoint routing is responsible for all dispatching decisions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-927">由於中介軟體會根據所選取的端點來套用原則，因此請務必在路由系統內制定可能影響分派或應用安全性原則的任何決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-927">Since the middleware applies policies based on the selected endpoint, it's important that any decision that can affect dispatching or the application of security policies is made inside the routing system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-928">執行端點委派時，會根據到目前為止所執行的要求處理，將 [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) 的屬性設定為適當的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-928">When the endpoint delegate is executed, the properties of [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) are set to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-929">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) 是「路由值」的字典，而路由值產生自路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-929">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) is a dictionary of *route values* produced from the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-930">這些值通常是透過將 URL 語彙基元化來決定，可以用來接受使用者輸入，或在應用程式內做出進一步的分派決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-930">These values are usually determined by tokenizing the URL and can be used to accept user input or to make further dispatching decisions inside the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-931">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 是其他資料的屬性包，而這些資料與相符路由相關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-931">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) is a property bag of additional data related to the matched route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-932">提供了 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> 來支援與每個路由建立關聯的狀態資料，因此應用程式可以依據符合哪一個路由來制定決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-932"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> are provided to support associating state data with each route so that the app can make decisions based on which route matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-933">這些是開發人員定義的值，**不會** 以任何方式影響路由的行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-933">These values are developer-defined and do **not** affect the behavior of routing in any way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-934">此外，儲藏在 [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 中的值可以是任何類型，對比之下，[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values) 則必須可轉換成字串或可從字串轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-934">Additionally, values stashed in [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) can be of any type, in contrast to [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), which must be convertible to and from strings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-935">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) 是成功符合要求的參與路由清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-935">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) is a list of the routes that took part in successfully matching the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-936">路由可以用巢狀方式置於彼此內部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-936">Routes can be nested inside of one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-937"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 屬性會透過導致產生相符項目的路由邏輯樹狀結構反映路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-937">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> property reflects the path through the logical tree of routes that resulted in a match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-938">一般而言，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 中的第一個項目是路由集合，應該用於產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-938">Generally, the first item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route collection and should be used for URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-939"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 中的最後一個項目是相符的路由處理常式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-939">The last item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route handler that matched.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation-with-linkgenerator"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-940">使用 LinkGenerator 產生 URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-940">URL generation with LinkGenerator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-941">URL 產生是路由可用來依據一組路由值建立 URL 路徑的處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-941">URL generation is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-942">這可讓您在端點和存取它們的 URL 之間建立邏輯分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-942">This allows for a logical separation between your endpoints and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-943">端點路由包含連結產生器 API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-943">Endpoint routing includes the Link Generator API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-944"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 是可從 [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection)取出的單一服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-944"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is a singleton service that can be retrieved from [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-945">您可以在執行要求內容外部使用此 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-945">The API can be used outside of the context of an executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-946">MVC 的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 及依賴 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 的情節 (例如[標籤協助程式](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro)、HTML 協助程式和[動作結果](xref:mvc/controllers/actions)) 均使用連結產生器來提供連結產生功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-946">MVC's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> and scenarios that rely on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, such as [Tag Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML Helpers, and [Action Results](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), use the link generator to provide link generating capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-947">連結產生器背後支援的概念為「位址」和「位址配置」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-947">The link generator is backed by the concept of an *address* and *address schemes*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-948">位址配置可讓您判斷應考慮用於連結產生的端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-948">An address scheme is a way of determining the endpoints that should be considered for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-949">例如，許多使用者熟悉的路由名稱和路由值案例 Razor 會實作為位址配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-949">For example, the route name and route values scenarios many users are familiar with from MVC/Razor Pages are implemented as an address scheme.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-950">連結產生器可以透過下列擴充方法，連結至 MVC/ Razor 頁面動作和頁面：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-950">The link generator can link to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages via the following extension methods:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByPage*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByPage*>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-951">這些方法的多載接受包含 `HttpContext` 的引數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-951">An overload of these methods accepts arguments that include the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-952">這些方法的功能等同於 `Url.Action` 和 `Url.Page`，但提供更多彈性和選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-952">These methods are functionally equivalent to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` but offer additional flexibility and options.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-953">`GetPath*` 方法與 `Url.Action` 和 `Url.Page` 最類似，因為它們會產生包含絕對路徑的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-953">The `GetPath*` methods are most similar to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` in that they generate a URI containing an absolute path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-954">`GetUri*` 方法一律會產生包含配置和主機的絕對 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-954">The `GetUri*` methods always generate an absolute URI containing a scheme and host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-955">接受 `HttpContext` 的方法會在執行要求的內容中產生 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-955">The methods that accept an `HttpContext` generate a URI in the context of the executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-956">除非遭到覆寫，否則會使用來自執行要求的環境路由值、URL 基底路徑、配置和主機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-956">The ambient route values, URL base path, scheme, and host from the executing request are used unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-957">呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 並指定一個位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-957"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is called with an address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-958">執行下列兩個步驟來產生 URI：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-958">Generating a URI occurs in two steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-959">將位址繫結至符合該位址的端點清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-959">An address is bound to a list of endpoints that match the address.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-960">評估每個端點的 `RoutePattern`，直到找到符合所提供值的路由模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-960">Each endpoint's `RoutePattern` is evaluated until a route pattern that matches the supplied values is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-961">產生的輸出會與提供給連結產生器的其他 URI 組件合併並傳回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-961">The resulting output is combined with the other URI parts supplied to the link generator and returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-962"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 提供的方法支援適用於任何位址類型的標準連結產生功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-962">The methods provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> support standard link generation capabilities for any type of address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-963">使用連結產生器的最便利方式是透過執行特定位址類型作業的擴充方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-963">The most convenient way to use the link generator is through extension methods that perform operations for a specific address type.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-964">擴充方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-964">Extension Method</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-965">說明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-965">Description</span></span>                                                         |
| ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-966">根據提供的值產生具有絕對路徑的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-966">Generates a URI with an absolute path based on the provided values.</span></span> |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetUriByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-967">根據提供的值產生絕對 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-967">Generates an absolute URI based on the provided values.</span></span>             |

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-968">注意呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 方法的下列影響：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-968">Pay attention to the following implications of calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> methods:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-969">使用 `GetUri*` 擴充方法，並注意應用程式組態不會驗證傳入要求的 `Host` 標頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-969">Use `GetUri*` extension methods with caution in an app configuration that doesn't validate the `Host` header of incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-970">如果傳入要求的 `Host` 標頭未經驗證，則可能將未受信任的要求輸入傳回檢視/頁面 URI 中的用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-970">If the `Host` header of incoming requests isn't validated, untrusted request input can be sent back to the client in URIs in a view/page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-971">建議所有生產應用程式將其伺服器設定為驗證 `Host` 標頭是否為已知有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-971">We recommend that all production apps configure their server to validate the `Host` header against known valid values.</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-972">使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>，並注意與 `Map` 或 `MapWhen` 搭配使用的中介軟體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-972">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> with caution in middleware in combination with `Map` or `MapWhen`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-973">`Map*` 會變更執行要求的基底路徑，這會影響連結產生的輸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-973">`Map*` changes the base path of the executing request, which affects the output of link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-974">所有的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API 都允許指定基底路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-974">All of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> APIs allow specifying a base path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-975">請一律指定空白基底路徑來恢復 `Map*` 對連結產生的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-975">Always specify an empty base path to undo `Map*`'s affect on link generation.</span></span>

## <a name="differences-from-earlier-versions-of-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-976">與舊版路由的差異</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-976">Differences from earlier versions of routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-977">ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由與 ASP.NET Core 中的舊版路由之間有一些差異：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-977">A few differences exist between endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later and earlier versions of routing in ASP.NET Core:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-978">端點路由系統不支援以 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 為基礎的擴充性，包括從 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 繼承。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-978">The endpoint routing system doesn't support <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based extensibility, including inheriting from <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-979">端點路由不支援 [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-979">Endpoint routing doesn't support [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-980">使用 2.1 [相容性版本](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) 繼續使用相容性填充碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-980">Use the 2.1 [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) to continue using the compatibility shim.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-981">端點路由與使用傳統路由時所產生 URI 大小寫的行為不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-981">Endpoint Routing has different behavior for the casing of generated URIs when using conventional routes.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-982">請考慮下列預設路由範本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-982">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-983">假設您使用下列路由來產生動作連結：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-983">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the following route:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-984">使用以 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 為基礎的路由，此程式碼會產生 `/blog/ReadPost/17` 的 URI，其遵守所提供路由值的大小寫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-984">With <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, this code generates a URI of `/blog/ReadPost/17`, which respects the casing of the provided route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-985">ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由會產生 `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" 為大寫)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-985">Endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" is capitalized).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-986">端點路由提供 `IOutboundParameterTransformer` 介面，可用來全域自訂此行為，或為對應 URL 套用不同的慣例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-986">Endpoint routing provides the `IOutboundParameterTransformer` interface that can be used to customize this behavior globally or to apply different conventions for mapping URLs.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-987">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[參數轉換器參考](#parameter-transformer-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-987">For more information, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-988">Razor當您嘗試連結至不存在的控制器/動作或頁面時，MVC/頁面與傳統路由所使用的連結產生會有不同的行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-988">Link Generation used by MVC/Razor Pages with conventional routes behaves differently when attempting to link to an controller/action or page that doesn't exist.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-989">請考慮下列預設路由範本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-989">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-990">假設您使用預設範本和下列程式碼來產生動作連結：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-990">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the default template with the following:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "Blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-991">使用以 `IRouter` 為基礎的路由，結果一律為 `/Blog/ReadPost/17`，即使 `BlogController` 不存在或沒有 `ReadPost` 動作方法也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-991">With `IRouter`-based routing, the result is always `/Blog/ReadPost/17`, even if the `BlogController` doesn't exist or doesn't have a `ReadPost` action method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-992">如預期，如果動作方法存在，則 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由會產生 `/Blog/ReadPost/17`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-992">As expected, endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` if the action method exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-993">不過，如果動作不存在，則端點路由會產生空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-993">*However, endpoint routing produces an empty string if the action doesn't exist.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-994">就概念而言，如果動作不存在，則端點路由不會假設端點存在。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-994">Conceptually, endpoint routing doesn't assume that the endpoint exists if the action doesn't exist.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-995">連結產生「環境值失效演算法」在搭配端點路由使用時會有不同的行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-995">The link generation *ambient value invalidation algorithm* behaves differently when used with endpoint routing.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-996">「環境值失效」是一種演算法，會從目前執行的要求 (環境值) 決定可用於連結產生作業的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-996">*Ambient value invalidation* is the algorithm that decides which route values from the currently executing request (the ambient values) can be used in link generation operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-997">傳統路由一律會在連結至其他動作時，使額外的路由值失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-997">Conventional routing always invalidated extra route values when linking to a different action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-998">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 版以前，屬性路由沒有此行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-998">Attribute routing didn't have this behavior prior to the release of ASP.NET Core 2.2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-999">在舊版的 ASP.NET Core 中，連結至使用相同路由參數名稱的其他動作會導致連結產生錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-999">In earlier versions of ASP.NET Core, links to another action that use the same route parameter names resulted in link generation errors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1000">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中，這兩種路由形式都會在連結至其他動作時使值失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1000">In ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, both forms of routing invalidate values when linking to another action.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1001">請考慮 ASP.NET Core 2.1 或更舊版本中的下列範例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1001">Consider the following example in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1002">連結至其他動作 (或其他頁面) 時，路由值可能會不適當地重複使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1002">When linking to another action (or another page), route values can be reused in undesirable ways.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1003">在 */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml* 中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1003">In */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id}"
  @Url.Page("/Login")
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1004">在 */Pages/Login.cshtml* 中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1004">In */Pages/Login.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id?}"
  ```
