  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1005">如果 URI 在 ASP.NET Core 2.1 或更舊版本中為 `/Store/Product/18`，則 `@Url.Page("/Login")` 在 Store/Info 頁面中產生的連結為 `/Login/18`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1005">If the URI is `/Store/Product/18` in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier, the link generated on the Store/Info page by `@Url.Page("/Login")` is `/Login/18`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1006">這會重複使用 `id` 值 18，即使連結目的地是完全不同的應用程式組件也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1006">The `id` value of 18 is reused, even though the link destination is different part of the app entirely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1007">`/Login` 頁面內容中的 `id` 路由值可能是使用者識別碼值，而不是市集產品識別碼值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1007">The `id` route value in the context of the `/Login` page is probably a user ID value, not a store product ID value.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1008">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由中，結果為 `/Login`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1008">In endpoint routing with ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, the result is `/Login`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1009">當連結的目的地是不同的動作或頁面時，不會重複使用環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1009">Ambient values aren't reused when the linked destination is a different action or page.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1010">往返路由參數語法：使用雙星號 (`**`) catch-all 參數語法時，斜線不會經過編碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1010">Round-tripping route parameter syntax: Forward slashes aren't encoded when using a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter syntax.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1011">在連結產生期間，除了斜線，路由系統還會對雙星號 (`**`) catch-all 參數 (例如 `{**myparametername}`) 中擷取的值進行編碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1011">During link generation, the routing system encodes the value captured in a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter (for example, `{**myparametername}`) except the forward slashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1012">ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中以 `IRouter` 為基礎的路由支援雙星號 catch-all。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1012">The double-asterisk catch-all is supported with `IRouter`-based routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1013">舊版 ASP.NET Core 中的單一星號 catch-all (`{*myparametername}`) 參數語法仍會受到支援，而且斜線會經過編碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1013">The single asterisk catch-all parameter syntax in prior versions of ASP.NET Core (`{*myparametername}`) remains supported, and forward slashes are encoded.</span></span>

  | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1014">路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1014">Route</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1015">以下列項目產生的連結：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1015">Link generated with</span></span><br>`Url.Action(new { category = "admin/products" })`&hellip; |
  | ------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------- |
  | `/search/{*page}`  | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1016">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (斜線會經過編碼)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1016">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (the forward slash is encoded)</span></span>             |
  | `/search/{**page}` | `/search/admin/products`                                              |

### <a name="middleware-example"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1017">中介軟體範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1017">Middleware example</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1018">在下列範例中，中介軟體使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API 建立列出市集產品的動作方法連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1018">In the following example, a middleware uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API to create link to an action method that lists store products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1019">應用程式中的任何類別都可以使用連結產生器，方法是將它插入類別並呼叫 `GenerateLink`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1019">Using the link generator by injecting it into a class and calling `GenerateLink` is available to any class in an app.</span></span>

```csharp
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing;

public class ProductsLinkMiddleware
{
    private readonly LinkGenerator _linkGenerator;

    public ProductsLinkMiddleware(RequestDelegate next, LinkGenerator linkGenerator)
    {
        _linkGenerator = linkGenerator;
    }

    public async Task InvokeAsync(HttpContext httpContext)
    {
        var url = _linkGenerator.GetPathByAction("ListProducts", "Store");

        httpContext.Response.ContentType = "text/plain";

        await httpContext.Response.WriteAsync($"Go to {url} to see our products.");
    }
}
```

### <a name="create-routes"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1020">建立路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1020">Create routes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1021">大部分的應用程式會藉由呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 或其中一個 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> 上定義的類似擴充方法來定建立路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1021">Most apps create routes by calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> or one of the similar extension methods defined on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1022">任何 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> 擴充方法都會建立 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 的執行個體，並將它新增至路由集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1022">Any of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> extension methods create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> and add it to the route collection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1023"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 不接受路由處理常式參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1023"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> doesn't accept a route handler parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1024"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 只會新增 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*> 所處理的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1024"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> only adds routes that are handled by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1025">若要深入了解 MVC 中的路由功能，請參閱 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1025">To learn more about routing in MVC, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1026">下列程式碼範例是典型 ASP.NET Core MVC 路由定義所使用的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 呼叫範例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1026">The following code example is an example of a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> call used by a typical ASP.NET Core MVC route definition:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1027">此範本會比對 URL 路徑，並擷取路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1027">This template matches a URL path and extracts the route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1028">例如，路徑 `/Products/Details/17` 會產生下列路由值：`{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1028">For example, the path `/Products/Details/17` generates the following route values: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1029">路由值是透過將 URL 路徑分割成區段，並比對每個區段與路由範本中的「路由參數」名稱來判定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1029">Route values are determined by splitting the URL path into segments and matching each segment with the *route parameter* name in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1030">路由參數為具名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1030">Route parameters are named.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1031">參數是透過以括弧 `{ ... }` 括住參數名稱來定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1031">The parameters defined by enclosing the parameter name in braces `{ ... }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1032">上述範本也可以比對 URL 路徑 `/` 並產生值 `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1032">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1033">發生這種情況是因為 `{controller}` 和 `{action}` 路由參數有預設值，而 `id` 路由參數為選擇性參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1033">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1034">路由參數名稱之後緊接著值的等號 (`=`) 會定義參數預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1034">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1035">路由參數名稱之後的問號 (`?`) 會定義選擇性參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1035">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1036">在路由相符時，具有預設值的路由參數一定會產生路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1036">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1037">如果沒有對應的 URL 路徑區段，選擇性參數不會產生路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1037">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there is no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1038">如需路由範本情節和語法的詳細描述，請參閱[路由範本參考](#route-template-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1038">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1039">在下列範例中，路由參數定義 `{id:int}` 會定義 `id` 路由參數的[路由條件約束](#route-constraint-reference)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1039">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1040">此範本會符合 `/Products/Details/17` 等 URL 路徑，但不符合 `/Products/Details/Apples`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1040">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1041">路由條件約束會實作 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>，並檢查路由值以進行驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1041">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1042">在此範例中，路由值 `id` 必須可以轉換為整數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1042">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1043">如需架構所提供之路由條件約束的說明，請參閱[路由條件約束參考](#route-constraint-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1043">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1044"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 的其他多載接受 `constraints`、`dataTokens` 和 `defaults` 的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1044">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1045">這些參數通常是用來傳遞匿名類型的物件，其中匿名類型的屬性名稱符合路由參數名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1045">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1046">下列 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 範例會建立對等的路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1046">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1047">對於簡單的路由而言，定義條件約束和預設的內嵌語法可能很方便。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1047">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1048">不過，內嵌語法不支援某些情節 (例如資料語彙基元)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1048">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1049">下列範例將示範一些其他情節：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1049">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{**article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1050">上述範本會比對 `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` 等 URL 路徑，並擷取值 `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1050">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1051">即使範本中沒有任何對應的路由參數，路由也會產生 `controller` 和 `action` 的預設路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1051">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1052">預設值可以在路由範本中指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1052">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1053">`article` 路由參數透過在路由參數名稱之前加上雙星號 (`**`) 來定義為 *catch-all*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1053">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an double asterisk (`**`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1054">全部擷取路由參數會擷取 URL 路徑的其餘部分，而且也可以符合空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1054">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1055">下列範例會新增路由條件約束和資料語彙基元：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1055">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1056">上述範本會比對 `/en-US/Products/5` 等 URL 路徑，並擷取值 `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` 和資料語彙基元 `{ locale = en-US }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1056">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![[區域變數] 視窗語彙基元](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1058">路由類別 URL 產生</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1058">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1059"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 類別也可以結合一組路由值與其路由範本來產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1059">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1060">這在邏輯上是比對 URL 路徑的反向處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1060">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1061">若要進一步了解 URL 產生，請假設您想要產生的 URL，並考慮路由範本將會如何比對該 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1061">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1062">產生的值為何？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1062">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1063">這與 URL 產生在 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 類別中的運作方式大致相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1063">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1064">下列範例使用一般 ASP.NET Core MVC 預設路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1064">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1065">路由值為 `{ controller = Products, action = List }` 時，會產生 URL `/Products/List`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1065">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1066">路由值會取代對應的路由參數，以形成 URL 路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1066">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1067">由於 `id` 是選擇性路由參數，因此沒有 `id` 值也可以成功產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1067">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1068">路由值為 `{ controller = Home, action = Index }` 時，會產生 URL `/`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1068">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1069">所提供的路由值符合預設值，因此可以放心地省略這些預設值對應的區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1069">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1070">這兩個產生的 URL 會使用下列路由定義 (`/Home/Index` 和 `/`) 反覆存取，並產生用來產生 URL 的相同路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1070">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1071">使用 ASP.NET Core MVC 的應用程式應該使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> 來產生 URL，而不是直接呼叫路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1071">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1072">如需 URL 產生的詳細資訊，請參閱 [URI 產生參考](#url-generation-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1072">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1073">使用路由中介軟體</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1073">Use Routing Middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1074">參考應用程式專案檔中的 [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App 中繼套件](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1074">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1075">在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中，將路由新增至服務容器：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1075">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1076">路由必須設定在 `Startup.Configure` 方法中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1076">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1077">範例應用程式使用下列 API：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1077">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1078"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>：僅符合 HTTP GET 要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1078"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>: Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1079">下表顯示使用指定 URL 的回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1079">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1080">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1080">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1081">回應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1081">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1082">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1082">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1083">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1083">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1084">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1084">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1085">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1085">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1086">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1086">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1087">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1087">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1088">要求失敗，沒有相符項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1088">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1089">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1089">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1090">要求失敗，僅符合 HTTP GET。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1090">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1091">要求失敗，沒有相符項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1091">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1092">架構會提供一組擴充方法來建立路由 (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1092">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1093">`Map[Verb]` 方法會使用條件約束，將路由限制為方法名稱中的 HTTP 指令動詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1093">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1094">如需範例，請參閱 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> 與 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1094">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1095">路由範本參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1095">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1096">大括弧 (`{ ... }`) 內的語彙基元定義路由相符時會繫結的「路由參數」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1096">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1097">您可以在路由區段中定義多個路由參數，但其必須以常值分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1097">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1098">例如，`{controller=Home}{action=Index}` 不是有效的路由，因為 `{controller}` 與 `{action}` 之間沒有任何常值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1098">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1099">這些路由參數必須有一個名稱，並且可以指定其他屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1099">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1100">路由參數之外的常值文字 (例如，`{id}`) 和路徑分隔符號 `/` 必須符合 URL 中的文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1100">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1101">文字比對會區分大小寫，並以 URL 路徑的已解碼表示法為基礎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1101">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1102">若要比對常值路由參數分隔符號 (`{` 或 `}`)，請重複字元 (`{{` 或 `}}`) 來將分隔符號逸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1102">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1103">URL 模式嘗試擷取具有選擇性副檔名的檔案名稱時，具有其他考量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1103">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1104">以範本 `files/{filename}.{ext?}` 為例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1104">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1105">當 `filename` 和 `ext` 都存在值時，就會填入這兩個值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1105">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1106">如果 URL 中只有 `filename` 存在值，由於結尾的句點 (`.`) 是選擇性項目，因此路由相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1106">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1107">下列 URL 符合此路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1107">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1108">您可以使用一個星號 (`*`) 或雙星號 (`**`) 作為路由參數的前置詞，以繫結至 URI 的其餘部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1108">You can use an asterisk (`*`) or double asterisk (`**`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1109">這稱為 *catch-all* 參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1109">These are called a *catch-all* parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1110">例如，`blog/{**slug}` 符合以 `/blog` 開頭且其後有任何值 (這會指派給 `slug` 路由值) 的所有 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1110">For example, `blog/{**slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1111">全部擷取參數也可以符合空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1111">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1112">當使用路由產生 URL (包括路徑分隔符號 (`/`) 字元) 時，catch-all 參數會逸出適當的字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1112">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1113">例如，路由值為 `{ path = "my/path" }` 的路由 `foo/{*path}` 會產生 `foo/my%2Fpath`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1113">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1114">請注意逸出的斜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1114">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1115">若要反覆存取路徑分隔符號字元，請使用 `**` 路由參數前置詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1115">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1116">具有 `{ path = "my/path" }` 的路由 `foo/{**path}` 會產生 `foo/my/path`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1116">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1117">路由參數可能有「預設值」，指定方法是在參數名稱之後指定預設值，並以等號 (`=`) 分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1117">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1118">例如，`{controller=Home}` 定義 `Home` 作為 `controller` 的預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1118">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1119">如果 URL 中沒有用於參數的任何值，則會使用預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1119">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1120">路由參數也可以設為選擇性，方法是在參數名稱結尾附加問號 (`?`)，如 `id?` 中所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1120">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1121">選擇性值與預設路由參數之間的差異在於，具有預設值的路由參數一定會產生值&mdash;選擇性參數只有在要求 URL 提供值時才會有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1121">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1122">路由參數可能具有條件約束，這些條件約束必須符合與 URL 繫結的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1122">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1123">在路由參數名稱之後新增分號 (`:`) 和條件約束名稱，即可指定路由參數的「內嵌條件約束」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1123">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1124">如果條件約束需要引數，這些引數會在條件約束名稱後面以括弧 (`(...)`) 括住。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1124">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1125">指定多個內嵌條件約束的方法是附加另一個冒號 (`:`) 和條件約束名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1125">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1126">條件約束名稱和引述會傳遞至 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> 服務來建立 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 的執行個體，以用於 URL 處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1126">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1127">例如，路由範本 `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` 指定具有引數 `10` 的 `minlength` 條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1127">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1128">如需路由條件約束詳細資訊和架構所提供的條件約束清單，請參閱[路由條件約束參考](#route-constraint-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1128">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1129">路由參數也可以具有參數轉換器，以在產生連結及根據 URL 比對動作和頁面時，轉換參數的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1129">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers, which transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1130">與條件約束類似，可以透過在路徑參數名稱後面新增冒號 (`:`) 和轉換器名稱，將參數轉換器內嵌新增至路徑參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1130">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a colon (`:`) and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1131">例如，路由範本 `blog/{article:slugify}` 會指定 `slugify` 轉換器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1131">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1132">如需參數轉換器的詳細資訊，請參閱[參數轉器參考](#parameter-transformer-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1132">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1133">下表示範範例路由範本及其行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1133">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1134">路由範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1134">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1135">範例比對 URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1135">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1136">要求 URI&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1136">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1137">只比對單一路徑 `/hello`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1137">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1138">比對並將 `Page` 設定為 `Home`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1138">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1139">比對並將 `Page` 設定為 `Contact`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1139">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1140">對應至 `Products` 控制器和 `List` 動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1140">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1141">對應至 `Products` 控制器和 `Details` 動作 (`id` 設定為 123)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1141">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1142">對應至 `Home` 控制器和 `Index` 方法 (會忽略 `id`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1142">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1143">使用範本通常是最簡單的路由方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1143">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1144">條件約束和預設值也可以在路由範本外部指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1144">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1145">啟用[記錄](xref:fundamentals/logging/index)以查看內建路由實作 (例如 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>) 如何符合要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1145">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1146">保留的路由名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1146">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1147">下列關鍵字是保留的名稱，不能用作路由名稱或參數：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1147">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1148">路由條件約束參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1148">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1149">路由條件約束執行時機是出現符合傳入 URL 的項目，並將 URL 路徑語彙基元化成路由值時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1149">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1150">路由條件約束通常會透過路由範本檢查相關聯的路由值，並對是否可接受值做出是/否決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1150">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1151">某些路由條件約束會使用路由值以外的資料，以考慮是否可以路由要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1151">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1152">例如，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> 可以依據其 HTTP 指令動詞接受或拒絕要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1152">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1153">條件約束可用於路由要求和連結產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1153">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1154">請勿針對 **輸入驗證** 使用條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1154">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1155">如果針對 **輸入驗證** 使用條件約束，則無效的輸入會導致產生「404 - 找不到」回應，而不是「400 - 錯誤要求」與適當的錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1155">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1156">路由條件約束會用來 **釐清** 類似的路由，而不是用來驗證特定路由的輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1156">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1157">下表示範範例路由條件約束及其預期行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1157">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1158">條件約束</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1158">Constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1159">範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1159">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1160">範例相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1160">Example matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1161">備註</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1161">Notes</span></span> |
|------------|---------|-----------------|-------|
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1162">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1162">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1163">符合任何整數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1163">Matches any integer.</span></span>|
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1164">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1164">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1165">符合 `true` 或 `false` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1165">Matches `true` or `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1166">不區分大小寫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1166">Case-insensitive.</span></span>|
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1167">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1167">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1168">符合非變異 `DateTime` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1168">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1169">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1169">See preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1170">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1170">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1171">符合非變異 `decimal` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1171">Matches a valid `decimal` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1172">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1172">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1173">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1173">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1174">符合非變異 `double` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1174">Matches a valid `double` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1175">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1175">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1176">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1176">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1177">符合非變異 `float` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1177">Matches a valid `float` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1178">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1178">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1179">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1179">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1180">符合有效的 `Guid` 值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1180">Matches a valid `Guid` value.</span></span>|
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1181">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1181">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1182">符合有效的 `long` 值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1182">Matches a valid `long` value.</span></span>|
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1183">字串必須至少有4個字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1183">String must be at least 4 characters.</span></span>|
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `MyFile` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1184">字串最多8個字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1184">String has maximum of 8 characters.</span></span>|
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1185">字串的長度必須剛好為12個字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1185">String must be exactly 12 characters long.</span></span>|
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1186">字串必須至少為8個字元，最多16個字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1186">String must be at least 8 and has maximum of 16 characters.</span></span>|
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1187">整數值必須至少為18。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1187">Integer value must be at least 18.</span></span>|
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1188">整數值最大值120。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1188">Integer value maximum of 120.</span></span>|
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1189">整數值必須至少為18，最大值為120。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1189">Integer value must be at least 18 and maximum of 120.</span></span>|
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1190">字串必須由一或多個字母字元組成 `a` - `z` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1190">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters `a`-`z`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1191">不區分大小寫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1191">Case-insensitive.</span></span>|
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1192">字串必須符合正則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1192">String must match the regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1193">請參閱定義正則運算式的秘訣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1193">See tips about defining a regular expression.</span></span>|
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1194">用來強制在 URL 產生期間存在非參數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1194">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation.</span></span>|

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1195">以冒號分隔的多個條件約束，可以套用至單一參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1195">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1196">例如，下列條件約束會將參數限制在 1 或更大的整數值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1196">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1197">確認 URL 可以轉換成 CLR 類型的路由條件約束 (例如 `int` 或 `DateTime`) 一律使用不因國別而異的文化特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1197">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1198">這些條件約束假設 URL 不可當地語系化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1198">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1199">架構提供的路由條件約束不會修改路由值中儲存的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1199">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1200">所有從 URL 剖析而來的路由值會儲存為字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1200">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1201">例如，`float` 條件約束會嘗試將路由值轉換成浮點數，但轉換的值只能用來確認它可以轉換成浮點數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1201">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1202">規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1202">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1203">ASP.NET Core 架構將 `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` 新增至規則運算式建構函式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1203">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1204">如需這些成員的說明，請參閱 <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1204">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1205">正則運算式使用的分隔符號和標記類似于路由和 c # 語言所使用的標記。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1205">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1206">規則運算式的語彙基元必須逸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1206">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1207">若要在路由中使用正則運算式 `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1207">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1208">運算式必須 `\` 在字串中提供以雙反斜線字元形式在原始程式碼中提供的單一反斜線字元 `\\` 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1208">The expression must have the single backslash `\` characters provided in the string as double backslash `\\` characters in the source code.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1209">正則運算式必須是我們才能將 `\\` `\` 字串 escape 字元換用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1209">The regular expression must us `\\` in order to escape the `\` string escape character.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1210">`\\`使用[逐字字串常](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)值時，不需要正則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1210">The regular expression doesn't require `\\` when using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1211">若要將路由參數分隔符號 `{` 、 `}` 、 `[` 、 `]` ，請將運算式中的字元 `{{` `}` `[[` `]]` （，）加倍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1211">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters `{`, `}`, `[`, `]`, double the characters in the expression `{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1212">下表顯示正則運算式和已轉義的版本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1212">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1213">規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1213">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1214">逸出的規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1214">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1215">路由中使用的正則運算式通常會以插入 `^` 號字元開頭，並符合字串的開始位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1215">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret `^` character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1216">運算式通常以貨幣符號 `$` 字元結尾，且字串的結尾相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1216">The expressions often end with the dollar sign `$` character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1217">`^` 和 `$` 字元可確保規則運算式符合整個路由參數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1217">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1218">若不使用 `^` 與 `$` 字元，規則運算式會比對字串內的所有部分字串，這通常不是您想要的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1218">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1219">下表提供範例，並說明它們符合或無法符合的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1219">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1220">運算是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1220">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1221">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1221">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1222">比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1222">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1223">註解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1223">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1224">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1224">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1225">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1225">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1226">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1226">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1227">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1227">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1228">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1228">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1229">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1229">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1230">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1230">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1231">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1231">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1232">符合運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1232">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1233">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1233">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1234">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1234">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1235">不區分大小寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1235">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1236">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1236">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1237">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1237">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1238">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1238">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1239">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1239">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1240">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1240">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1241">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1241">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1242">如需規則運算式語法的詳細資訊，請參閱 [.NET Framework 規則運算式](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1242">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1243">若要將參數限制為一組已知的可能值，請使用規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1243">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1244">例如，`{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` 只會將 `action` 路由值與 `list`、`get` 或 `create` 相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1244">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1245">如果已傳入條件約束字典，字串 `^(list|get|create)$` 則是對等項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1245">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1246">已傳入條件約束字典 (未內嵌在範本內) 的條件約束，即使不符合其中一個已知的條件約束，也會被視為規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1246">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1247">自訂路由條件約束</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1247">Custom route constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1248">除了內建的路由限制式之外，自訂路由限制式也可以透過實作 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 介面來建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1248">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1249"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 介面包含單一方法 `Match`，此方法會在滿足限制式時傳回 `true`，否則會傳回 `false`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1249">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1250">若要使用自訂 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>，路由限制式型別必須必須向應用程式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> (在應用程式的服務容器中) 註冊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1250">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1251"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 是一個目錄，它將路由限制式機碼對應到可驗證那些限制式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 實作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1251">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1252">更新應用程式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 時，可在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中於進行 [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) 呼叫時更新，或透過使用 `services.Configure<RouteOptions>` 直接設定 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> 來更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1252">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1253">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1253">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1254">限制式接著能以一般方式套用到路由 (使用註冊限制式型別時使用名稱)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1254">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1255">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1255">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1256">參數轉換器參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1256">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1257">參數轉換程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1257">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1258">會在為 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 產生連結時執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1258">Execute when generating a link for a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1259">實作 `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1259">Implement `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1260">是使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 進行設定的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1260">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1261">採用參數的路由值，並將它轉換為新的字串值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1261">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1262">導致在所產生連結中使用已轉換的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1262">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1263">例如，具有 `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` 之路由模式 `blog\{article:slugify}` 中的自訂 `slugify` 參數轉換器，會產生 `blog\my-test-article`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1263">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1264">若要在路由模式中使用參數轉換器，請先在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 進行設定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1264">To use a parameter transformer in a route pattern, configure it first using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    // Replace the type and the name used to refer to it with your own
    // IOutboundParameterTransformer implementation
    options.ConstraintMap["slugify"] = typeof(SlugifyParameterTransformer);
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1265">架構會使用參數轉換器來轉換端點解析的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1265">Parameter transformers are used by the framework to transform the URI where an endpoint resolves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1266">例如，ASP.NET Core MVC 會使用參數轉換器，轉換用於比對 `area`、`controller`、`action` 和 `page` 的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1266">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC uses parameter transformers to transform the route value used to match an `area`, `controller`, `action`, and `page`.</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller:slugify=Home}/{action:slugify=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1267">使用上述的路由，動作 `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll` 會與URI `/subscription-management/get-all` 比對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1267">With the preceding route, the action `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll` is matched with the URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1268">參數轉換器不會變更用來產生連結的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1268">A parameter transformer doesn't change the route values used to generate a link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1269">例如，`Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` 會輸出 `/subscription-management/get-all`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1269">For example, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` outputs `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1270">ASP.NET Core 針對搭配產生的路由使用參數轉換程式提供了 API 慣例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1270">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using a parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1271">ASP.NET Core MVC 有 `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API 慣例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1271">ASP.NET Core MVC has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1272">此慣例會將所指定參數轉換程式套用到應用程式中的所有屬性路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1272">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1273">參數轉換程式會在被取代時轉換屬性路由語彙基元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1273">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1274">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用參數轉換程式自訂語彙基元取代](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1274">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1275">Razor 頁面具有 `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API 慣例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1275">Razor Pages has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1276">此慣例會將指定的參數轉換器套用至所有自動探索到的 Razor 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1276">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1277">參數轉換程式會轉換頁面路由的資料夾和檔案名區段 Razor 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1277">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1278">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用參數轉換程式自訂頁面路由](xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1278">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1279">URL 產生參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1279">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1280">下列範例示範如何在指定路由值字典和 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection> 的情況下產生路由的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1280">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1281">在上述範例的結尾產生的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> 是 `/package/create/123`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1281">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1282">字典提供「追蹤套件路由」範本 `package/{operation}/{id}` 的 `operation` 和 `id` 路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1282">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1283">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用路由中介軟體](#use-routing-middleware)一節或[範例應用程式](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples)中的範例程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1283">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1284"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> 建構函式的第二個參數是「環境值」的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1284">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1285">環境值便於使用，因為它們會限制開發人員必須在要求內容中指定的值數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1285">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1286">目前要求的目前路由值被視為用於連結產生的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1286">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1287">在 ASP.NET Core MVC 應用程式 `HomeController` 的 `About` 動作中，您不需要指定控制器路由值以連結到 `Index` 動作&mdash;會使用 `Home` 的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1287">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1288">不符合參數的環境值會予以忽略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1288">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1289">當明確提供的值覆寫環境值時，也會忽略環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1289">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1290">URL 中的比對是從左到右。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1290">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1291">明確提供但不符合路由區段的值會新增至查詢字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1291">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1292">下表顯示使用路由範本 `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` 時的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1292">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1293">環境值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1293">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1294">明確值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1294">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1295">結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1295">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1296">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1296">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1297">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1297">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1298">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1298">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1299">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1299">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1300">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1300">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1301">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1301">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1302">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1302">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1303">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1303">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1304">如果路由具有未對應至參數的預設值，且該值會明確提供，它必須符合預設值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1304">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1305">連結產生只有在提供了 `controller` 與 `action` 的相符值時，才會產生此路由的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1305">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1306">複雜區段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1306">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1307">複雜區段 (例如，`[Route("/x{token}y")]`) 會透過以非窮盡的方式，由右至左比對常值來處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1307">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1308">請參閱[此程式碼](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/v2.2.13/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)以了解如何比對複雜區段的詳細解釋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1308">See [this code](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/v2.2.13/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1309">[程式法範例](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/v2.2.13/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)不是由 ASP.NET Core 使用，但它提供一個好的複雜區段解釋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1309">The [code sample](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/v2.2.13/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>
<!-- While that code is no longer used by ASP.NET Core for complex segment matching, it provides a good match to the current algorithm. The [current code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/91514c9af7e0f4c44029b51f05a01c6fe4c96e4c/src/Http/Routing/src/Matching/DfaMatcherBuilder.cs#L227-L244) is too abstracted from matching to be useful for understanding complex segment matching.
-->

::: moniker-end

::: moniker range="< aspnetcore-2.2"
