<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1310">路由功能負責將要求 URI 對應至路由處理常式，並分派傳入要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1310">Routing is responsible for mapping request URIs to route handlers and dispatching an incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1311">路由定義於應用程式，並在該應用程式啟動時進行設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1311">Routes are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1312">路由可以選擇性地從要求中所包含的 URL 擷取值，然後這些值就可用於處理要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1312">A route can optionally extract values from the URL contained in the request, and these values can then be used for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1313">使用應用程式中已設定的路由，路由功能將能夠產生對應至路由處理常式的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1313">Using configured routes from the app, routing is able to generate URLs that map to route handlers.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1314">若要使用 ASP.NET Core 2.1 中的最新路由情節，請將[相容性版本](xref:mvc/compatibility-version)指定為 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中的 MVC 服務註冊：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1314">To use the latest routing scenarios in ASP.NET Core 2.1, specify the [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) to the MVC services registration in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddMvc()
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1);
```

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1315">本文件涵蓋低階的 ASP.NET Core 路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1315">This document covers low-level ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1316">如需 ASP.NET Core MVC 路由的資訊，請參閱 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1316">For information on ASP.NET Core MVC routing, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1317">如需頁面中路由慣例的詳細資訊 Razor ，請參閱 <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1317">For information on routing conventions in Razor Pages, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1318">[查看或下載範例程式碼](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([如何下載](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1318">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1319">路由的基本概念</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1319">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1320">大部分應用程式都應該選擇基本的描述性路由傳送配置，讓 URL 可讀且有意義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1320">Most apps should choose a basic and descriptive routing scheme so that URLs are readable and meaningful.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1321">預設慣例路由 `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1321">The default conventional route `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1322">支援基本的描述性路由配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1322">Supports a basic and descriptive routing scheme.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1323">適合作為 UI 型應用程式的起點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1323">Is a useful starting point for UI-based apps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1324">在特殊情況下，開發人員通常會使用[屬性路由](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing)或專屬的慣例路由，新增額外的簡潔路由到應用程式的高流量區域 (例如，部落格和電子商務端點)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1324">Developers commonly add additional terse routes to high-traffic areas of an app in specialized situations (for example, blog and ecommerce endpoints) using [attribute routing](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) or dedicated conventional routes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1325">Web API 應該使用屬性路由傳送來將應用程式功能模型建構為作業由 HTTP 指令動詞代表的資源集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1325">Web APIs should use attribute routing to model the app's functionality as a set of resources where operations are represented by HTTP verbs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1326">這表示相同邏輯資源上的許多作業 (例如，GET、POST) 都會使用相同的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1326">This means that many operations (for example, GET, POST) on the same logical resource will use the same URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1327">屬性路由提供仔細設計 API 公用端點配置所需的控制層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1327">Attribute routing provides a level of control that's needed to carefully design an API's public endpoint layout.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1328">Razor 頁面應用程式會使用預設的傳統路由，在應用程式的 *Pages* 資料夾中提供命名資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1328">Razor Pages apps use default conventional routing to serve named resources in the *Pages* folder of an app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1329">有其他慣例可讓您自訂 Razor 頁面路由行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1329">Additional conventions are available that allow you to customize Razor Pages routing behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1330">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 <xref:razor-pages/index> 和 <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1330">For more information, see <xref:razor-pages/index> and <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1331">URL 產生支援允許在不需要硬式編碼的 URL 來連結應用程式的情況下開發應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1331">URL generation support allows the app to be developed without hard-coding URLs to link the app together.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1332">這項支援可讓您從基本路由設定開始，並在決定應用程式資源配置之後修改路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1332">This support allows for starting with a basic routing configuration and modifying the routes after the app's resource layout is determined.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1333">路由會使用的路由 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 執行：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1333">Routing uses routes implementations of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> to:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1334">將傳入要求對應至「路由處理常式」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1334">Map incoming requests to *route handlers*.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1335">產生用於回應的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1335">Generate the URLs used in responses.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1336">根據預設，應用程式有一個路由集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1336">By default, an app has a single collection of routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1337">當要求抵達時，集合中的路由會依其存在於集合的順序進行處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1337">When a request arrives, the routes in the collection are processed in the order that they exist in the collection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1338">此架構會嘗試對集合中的每個路由呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> 方法，藉以比對傳入要求 URL 與集合中的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1338">The framework attempts to match an incoming request URL to a route in the collection by calling the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> method on each route in the collection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1339">回應可以根據路由資訊使用路由來產生 URL (例如，針對重新導向或連結)，因此避免硬式編碼的 URL，這有助於可維護性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1339">A response can use routing to generate URLs (for example, for redirection or links) based on route information and thus avoid hard-coded URLs, which helps maintainability.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1340">路由系統具有下列特性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1340">The routing system has the following characteristics:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1341">使用路由範本語法以 Token 化路由參數來定義路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1341">Route template syntax is used to define routes with tokenized route parameters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1342">允許傳統式和屬性式端點組態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1342">Conventional-style and attribute-style endpoint configuration is permitted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1343"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 可用來判斷 URL 參數是否包含對指定端點條件約束有效的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1343"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> is used to determine whether a URL parameter contains a valid value for a given endpoint constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1344">應用程式模型（例如 MVC/ Razor Pages）會註冊其所有路由，其具有可預測的路由案例執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1344">App models, such as MVC/Razor Pages, register all of their routes, which have a predictable implementation of routing scenarios.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1345">回應可以根據路由資訊使用路由來產生 URL (例如，針對重新導向或連結)，因此避免硬式編碼的 URL，這有助於可維護性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1345">A response can use routing to generate URLs (for example, for redirection or links) based on route information and thus avoid hard-coded URLs, which helps maintainability.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1346">URL 是根據支援任意擴充性的路由所產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1346">URL generation is based on routes, which support arbitrary extensibility.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1347"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 提供方法來建立 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1347"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> offers methods to build URLs.</span></span>
<!-- fix [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) -->
<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1348">路由會透過 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> 類別連線到[中介軟體](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index)管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1348">Routing is connected to the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1349">[ASP.NET CORE mvc](xref:mvc/overview) 會將路由新增至中介軟體管線，作為其設定的一部分，並處理 MVC 和 Razor 頁面應用程式中的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1349">[ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) adds routing to the middleware pipeline as part of its configuration and handles routing in MVC and Razor Pages apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1350">若要了解如何使用路由作為獨立元件，請參閱[使用路由中介軟體](#use-routing-middleware)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1350">To learn how to use routing as a standalone component, see the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section.</span></span>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1351">URL 比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1351">URL matching</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1352">URL 比對是路由用來將傳入要求分派給「處理常式」的處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1352">URL matching is the process by which routing dispatches an incoming request to a *handler*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1353">這個處理序是基於 URL 路徑中的資料，但是可以擴展為考慮要求中的任何資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1353">This process is based on data in the URL path but can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1354">分派要求給不同處理常式的能力，是調整應用程式大小和複雜度的關鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1354">The ability to dispatch requests to separate handlers is key to scaling the size and complexity of an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1355">傳入要求將進入 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware>，而後者會依序在每個路由上呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> 方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1355">Incoming requests enter the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware>, which calls the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> method on each route in sequence.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1356"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 執行個體可將 [RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler*) 設定為非 Null 的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>，來選擇是否要「處理」要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1356">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> instance chooses whether to *handle* the request by setting the [RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler*) to a non-null <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1357">如果路由為要求設定了處理常式，則路由處理會停止，且會叫用該處理常式來處理要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1357">If a route sets a handler for the request, route processing stops, and the handler is invoked to process the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1358">如果找不到處理要求的路由處理常式，中介軟體會將要求傳遞給要求管線中的下一個中介軟體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1358">If no route handler is found to process the request, the middleware hands the request off to the next middleware in the request pipeline.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1359"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> 的主要輸入是與目前要求建立關聯的 [RouteContext.HttpContext](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.HttpContext*)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1359">The primary input to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> is the [RouteContext.HttpContext](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.HttpContext*) associated with the current request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1360">[RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler) 和 [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData*) 是在比對路由之後設定的輸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1360">The [RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler) and [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData*) are outputs set after a route is matched.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1361">呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> 的比對也會根據到目前為止所執行的要求處理，將 [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) 的屬性設定為適當的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1361">A match that calls <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> also sets the properties of the [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1362">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) 是「路由值」的字典，而路由值產生自路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1362">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) is a dictionary of *route values* produced from the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1363">這些值通常是透過將 URL 語彙基元化來決定，可以用來接受使用者輸入，或在應用程式內做出進一步的分派決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1363">These values are usually determined by tokenizing the URL and can be used to accept user input or to make further dispatching decisions inside the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1364">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 是其他資料的屬性包，而這些資料與相符路由相關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1364">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) is a property bag of additional data related to the matched route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1365">提供了 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> 來支援與每個路由建立關聯的狀態資料，因此應用程式可以依據符合哪一個路由來制定決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1365"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> are provided to support associating state data with each route so that the app can make decisions based on which route matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1366">這些是開發人員定義的值，**不會** 以任何方式影響路由的行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1366">These values are developer-defined and do **not** affect the behavior of routing in any way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1367">此外，儲藏在 [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 中的值可以是任何類型，對比之下，[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values) 則必須可轉換成字串或可從字串轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1367">Additionally, values stashed in [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) can be of any type, in contrast to [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), which must be convertible to and from strings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1368">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) 是成功符合要求的參與路由清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1368">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) is a list of the routes that took part in successfully matching the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1369">路由可以用巢狀方式置於彼此內部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1369">Routes can be nested inside of one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1370"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 屬性會透過導致產生相符項目的路由邏輯樹狀結構反映路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1370">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> property reflects the path through the logical tree of routes that resulted in a match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1371">一般而言，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 中的第一個項目是路由集合，應該用於產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1371">Generally, the first item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route collection and should be used for URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1372"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 中的最後一個項目是相符的路由處理常式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1372">The last item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route handler that matched.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1373">URL 產生</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1373">URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1374">URL 產生是路由可用來依據一組路由值建立 URL 路徑的處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1374">URL generation is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1375">這可讓您在路由處理常式和存取它們的 URL 之間建立邏輯分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1375">This allows for a logical separation between route handlers and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1376">URL 產生遵循類似的反覆執行處理序，但開頭是呼叫路由集合 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> 方法的使用者或架構程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1376">URL generation follows a similar iterative process, but it starts with user or framework code calling into the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> method of the route collection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1377">每個「路由」會依序呼叫其 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> 方法，直到傳回非 Null 的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> 為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1377">Each *route* has its <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> method called in sequence until a non-null <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> is returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1378"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> 的主要輸入是：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1378">The primary inputs to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> are:</span></span>

* [<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1379">VirtualPathContext.HttpContext</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1379">VirtualPathContext.HttpContext</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.HttpContext)
* [<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1380">VirtualPathContext.Values</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1380">VirtualPathContext.Values</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values)
* [<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1381">VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1381">VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues)

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1382">路由主要使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> 和 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> 所提供的路由值，以決定是否可能產生 URL，以及要包含哪些值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1382">Routes primarily use the route values provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> to decide whether it's possible to generate a URL and what values to include.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1383"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> 是比對目前要求所產生的路由值集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1383">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> are the set of route values that were produced from matching the current request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1384">相反地，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> 是指定如何產生目前作業所需之 URL 的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1384">In contrast, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> are the route values that specify how to generate the desired URL for the current operation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1385">提供了 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.HttpContext>，以防路由應該取得服務或與目前內容建立關聯的其他資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1385">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.HttpContext> is provided in case a route should obtain services or additional data associated with the current context.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1386">將 [VirtualPathContext.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values*) 視為 [VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues*) 的覆寫項目集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1386">Think of [VirtualPathContext.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values*) as a set of overrides for the [VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1387">URL 產生會嘗試重複使用來自目前要求的路由值，讓您使用相同路由或路由值產生連結的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1387">URL generation attempts to reuse route values from the current request to generate URLs for links using the same route or route values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1388"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> 的輸出是 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1388">The output of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> is a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1389"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> 是 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData> 的平行處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1389"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> is a parallel of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1390"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> 包含用於輸出 URL 的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath>，以及一些路由應該設定的其他屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1390"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> contains the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> for the output URL and some additional properties that should be set by the route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1391">[VirtualPathData.VirtualPath](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath*) 屬性包含路由所產生的「虛擬路徑」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1391">The [VirtualPathData.VirtualPath](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath*) property contains the *virtual path* produced by the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1392">視您需求的不同，可能需要進一步處理路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1392">Depending on your needs, you may need to process the path further.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1393">如果您想要以 HTML 呈現產生的 URL，請在前面加上應用程式的基底路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1393">If you want to render the generated URL in HTML, prepend the base path of the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1394">[VirtualPathData.Router](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.Router*) 是成功產生 URL 的路由參考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1394">The [VirtualPathData.Router](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.Router*) is a reference to the route that successfully generated the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1395">[VirtualPathData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.DataTokens*) 屬性是其他資料的字典，而這些資料與產生 URL 的路由相關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1395">The [VirtualPathData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.DataTokens*) properties is a dictionary of additional data related to the route that generated the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1396">這是 [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 的平行處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1396">This is the parallel of [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*).</span></span>

### <a name="create-routes"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1397">建立路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1397">Create routes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1398">路由提供 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 類別作為 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 的標準實作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1398">Routing provides the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class as the standard implementation of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1399">在呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> 時，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 會使用「路由範本」語法來定義將比對 URL 路徑的模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1399"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> uses the *route template* syntax to define patterns to match against the URL path when <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> is called.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1400">在呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> 時，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 會使用相同的路由範本來產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1400"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> uses the same route template to generate a URL when <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> is called.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1401">大部分的應用程式會藉由呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 或其中一個 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> 上定義的類似擴充方法來定建立路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1401">Most apps create routes by calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> or one of the similar extension methods defined on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1402">任何 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> 擴充方法都會建立 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 的執行個體，並將它新增至路由集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1402">Any of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> extension methods create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> and add it to the route collection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1403"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 不接受路由處理常式參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1403"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> doesn't accept a route handler parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1404"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 只會新增 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*> 所處理的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1404"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> only adds routes that are handled by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1405">預設處理常式為 `IRouter`，該處理常式可能無法處理要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1405">The default handler is an `IRouter`, and the handler might not handle the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1406">例如，ASP.NET Core MVC 通常會設定為預設處理常式，只處理符合可用控制器和動作的要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1406">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC is typically configured as a default handler that only handles requests that match an available controller and action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1407">若要深入了解 MVC 中的路由功能，請參閱 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1407">To learn more about routing in MVC, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1408">下列程式碼範例是典型 ASP.NET Core MVC 路由定義所使用的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 呼叫範例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1408">The following code example is an example of a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> call used by a typical ASP.NET Core MVC route definition:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1409">此範本會比對 URL 路徑，並擷取路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1409">This template matches a URL path and extracts the route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1410">例如，路徑 `/Products/Details/17` 會產生下列路由值：`{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1410">For example, the path `/Products/Details/17` generates the following route values: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1411">路由值是透過將 URL 路徑分割成區段，並比對每個區段與路由範本中的「路由參數」名稱來判定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1411">Route values are determined by splitting the URL path into segments and matching each segment with the *route parameter* name in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1412">路由參數為具名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1412">Route parameters are named.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1413">參數是透過以括弧 `{ ... }` 括住參數名稱來定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1413">The parameters defined by enclosing the parameter name in braces `{ ... }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1414">上述範本也可以比對 URL 路徑 `/` 並產生值 `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1414">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1415">發生這種情況是因為 `{controller}` 和 `{action}` 路由參數有預設值，而 `id` 路由參數為選擇性參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1415">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1416">路由參數名稱之後緊接著值的等號 (`=`) 會定義參數預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1416">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1417">路由參數名稱之後的問號 (`?`) 會定義選擇性參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1417">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1418">在路由相符時，具有預設值的路由參數一定會產生路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1418">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1419">如果沒有對應的 URL 路徑區段，選擇性參數不會產生路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1419">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there is no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1420">如需路由範本情節和語法的詳細描述，請參閱[路由範本參考](#route-template-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1420">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1421">在下列範例中，路由參數定義 `{id:int}` 會定義 `id` 路由參數的[路由條件約束](#route-constraint-reference)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1421">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1422">此範本會符合 `/Products/Details/17` 等 URL 路徑，但不符合 `/Products/Details/Apples`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1422">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1423">路由條件約束會實作 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>，並檢查路由值以進行驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1423">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1424">在此範例中，路由值 `id` 必須可以轉換為整數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1424">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1425">如需架構所提供之路由條件約束的說明，請參閱[路由條件約束參考](#route-constraint-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1425">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1426"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 的其他多載接受 `constraints`、`dataTokens` 和 `defaults` 的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1426">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1427">這些參數通常是用來傳遞匿名類型的物件，其中匿名類型的屬性名稱符合路由參數名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1427">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1428">下列 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 範例會建立對等的路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1428">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1429">對於簡單的路由而言，定義條件約束和預設的內嵌語法可能很方便。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1429">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1430">不過，內嵌語法不支援某些情節 (例如資料語彙基元)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1430">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1431">下列範例將示範一些其他情節：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1431">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{*article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1432">上述範本會比對 `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` 等 URL 路徑，並擷取值 `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1432">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1433">即使範本中沒有任何對應的路由參數，路由也會產生 `controller` 和 `action` 的預設路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1433">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1434">預設值可以在路由範本中指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1434">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1435">`article` 路由參數透過在路由參數名稱之前加上一個星號 (`*`) 來定義為 *catch-all*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1435">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an asterisk (`*`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1436">全部擷取路由參數會擷取 URL 路徑的其餘部分，而且也可以符合空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1436">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1437">下列範例會新增路由條件約束和資料語彙基元：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1437">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1438">上述範本會比對 `/en-US/Products/5` 等 URL 路徑，並擷取值 `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` 和資料語彙基元 `{ locale = en-US }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1438">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![[區域變數] 視窗語彙基元](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1440">路由類別 URL 產生</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1440">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1441"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 類別也可以結合一組路由值與其路由範本來產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1441">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1442">這在邏輯上是比對 URL 路徑的反向處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1442">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1443">若要進一步了解 URL 產生，請假設您想要產生的 URL，並考慮路由範本將會如何比對該 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1443">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1444">產生的值為何？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1444">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1445">這與 URL 產生在 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 類別中的運作方式大致相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1445">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1446">下列範例使用一般 ASP.NET Core MVC 預設路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1446">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1447">路由值為 `{ controller = Products, action = List }` 時，會產生 URL `/Products/List`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1447">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1448">路由值會取代對應的路由參數，以形成 URL 路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1448">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1449">由於 `id` 是選擇性路由參數，因此沒有 `id` 值也可以成功產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1449">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1450">路由值為 `{ controller = Home, action = Index }` 時，會產生 URL `/`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1450">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1451">所提供的路由值符合預設值，因此可以放心地省略這些預設值對應的區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1451">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1452">這兩個產生的 URL 會使用下列路由定義 (`/Home/Index` 和 `/`) 反覆存取，並產生用來產生 URL 的相同路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1452">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1453">使用 ASP.NET Core MVC 的應用程式應該使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> 來產生 URL，而不是直接呼叫路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1453">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1454">如需 URL 產生的詳細資訊，請參閱 [URI 產生參考](#url-generation-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1454">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1455">使用路由中介軟體</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1455">Use routing middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1456">參考應用程式專案檔中的 [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App 中繼套件](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1456">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1457">在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中，將路由新增至服務容器：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1457">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1458">路由必須設定在 `Startup.Configure` 方法中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1458">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1459">範例應用程式使用下列 API：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1459">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1460"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>：僅符合 HTTP GET 要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1460"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>: Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1461">下表顯示使用指定 URL 的回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1461">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1462">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1462">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1463">回應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1463">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1464">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1464">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1465">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1465">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1466">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1466">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1467">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1467">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1468">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1468">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1469">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1469">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1470">要求失敗，沒有相符項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1470">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1471">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1471">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1472">要求失敗，僅符合 HTTP GET。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1472">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1473">要求失敗，沒有相符項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1473">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1474">如果您要設定單一路由，請呼叫傳入 `IRouter` 執行個體的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1474">If you're configuring a single route, call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passing in an `IRouter` instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1475">您不需要使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1475">You won't need to use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1476">架構會提供一組擴充方法來建立路由 (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1476">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1477">其中一些列出的方法 (例如 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>) 需要 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1477">Some of listed methods, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, require a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1478">路由相符時，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> 會作為「路由處理常式」使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1478">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> is used as the *route handler* when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1479">此系列中的其他方法允許設定中介軟體管線，以作為路由處理常式使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1479">Other methods in this family allow configuring a middleware pipeline for use as the route handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1480">如果 `Map*` 方法不接受處理常式 (例如 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>)，則會使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1480">If the `Map*` method doesn't accept a handler, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, it uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1481">`Map[Verb]` 方法會使用條件約束，將路由限制為方法名稱中的 HTTP 指令動詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1481">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1482">如需範例，請參閱 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> 與 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1482">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1483">路由範本參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1483">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1484">大括弧 (`{ ... }`) 內的語彙基元定義路由相符時會繫結的「路由參數」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1484">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1485">您可以在路由區段中定義多個路由參數，但其必須以常值分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1485">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1486">例如，`{controller=Home}{action=Index}` 不是有效的路由，因為 `{controller}` 與 `{action}` 之間沒有任何常值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1486">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1487">這些路由參數必須有一個名稱，並且可以指定其他屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1487">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1488">路由參數之外的常值文字 (例如，`{id}`) 和路徑分隔符號 `/` 必須符合 URL 中的文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1488">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1489">文字比對會區分大小寫，並以 URL 路徑的已解碼表示法為基礎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1489">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1490">若要比對常值路由參數分隔符號 (`{` 或 `}`)，請重複字元 (`{{` 或 `}}`) 來將分隔符號逸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1490">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1491">URL 模式嘗試擷取具有選擇性副檔名的檔案名稱時，具有其他考量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1491">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1492">以範本 `files/{filename}.{ext?}` 為例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1492">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1493">當 `filename` 和 `ext` 都存在值時，就會填入這兩個值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1493">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1494">如果 URL 中只有 `filename` 存在值，由於結尾的句點 (`.`) 是選擇性項目，因此路由相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1494">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1495">下列 URL 符合此路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1495">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1496">您可以使用星號 (`*`) 作為路由參數的前置詞，以繫結至 URI 的其餘部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1496">You can use the asterisk (`*`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1497">這稱為「全部擷取」參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1497">This is called a *catch-all* parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1498">例如，`blog/{*slug}` 符合以 `/blog` 開頭且其後有任何值 (這會指派給 `slug` 路由值) 的所有 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1498">For example, `blog/{*slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1499">全部擷取參數也可以符合空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1499">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1500">當使用路由產生 URL (包括路徑分隔符號 (`/`) 字元) 時，catch-all 參數會逸出適當的字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1500">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1501">例如，路由值為 `{ path = "my/path" }` 的路由 `foo/{*path}` 會產生 `foo/my%2Fpath`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1501">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1502">請注意逸出的斜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1502">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1503">路由參數可能有「預設值」，指定方法是在參數名稱之後指定預設值，並以等號 (`=`) 分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1503">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1504">例如，`{controller=Home}` 定義 `Home` 作為 `controller` 的預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1504">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1505">如果 URL 中沒有用於參數的任何值，則會使用預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1505">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1506">路由參數也可以設為選擇性，方法是在參數名稱結尾附加問號 (`?`)，如 `id?` 中所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1506">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1507">選擇性值與預設路由參數之間的差異在於，具有預設值的路由參數一定會產生值&mdash;選擇性參數只有在要求 URL 提供值時才會有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1507">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1508">路由參數可能具有條件約束，這些條件約束必須符合與 URL 繫結的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1508">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1509">在路由參數名稱之後新增分號 (`:`) 和條件約束名稱，即可指定路由參數的「內嵌條件約束」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1509">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1510">如果條件約束需要引數，這些引數會在條件約束名稱後面以括弧 (`(...)`) 括住。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1510">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1511">指定多個內嵌條件約束的方法是附加另一個冒號 (`:`) 和條件約束名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1511">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1512">條件約束名稱和引述會傳遞至 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> 服務來建立 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 的執行個體，以用於 URL 處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1512">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1513">例如，路由範本 `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` 指定具有引數 `10` 的 `minlength` 條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1513">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1514">如需路由條件約束詳細資訊和架構所提供的條件約束清單，請參閱[路由條件約束參考](#route-constraint-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1514">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1515">下表示範範例路由範本及其行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1515">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1516">路由範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1516">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1517">範例比對 URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1517">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1518">要求 URI&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1518">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1519">只比對單一路徑 `/hello`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1519">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1520">比對並將 `Page` 設定為 `Home`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1520">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1521">比對並將 `Page` 設定為 `Contact`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1521">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1522">對應至 `Products` 控制器和 `List` 動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1522">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1523">對應至 `Products` 控制器和 `Details` 動作 (`id` 設定為 123)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1523">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1524">對應至 `Home` 控制器和 `Index` 方法 (會忽略 `id`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1524">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1525">使用範本通常是最簡單的路由方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1525">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1526">條件約束和預設值也可以在路由範本外部指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1526">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1527">啟用[記錄](xref:fundamentals/logging/index)以查看內建路由實作 (例如 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>) 如何符合要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1527">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1528">路由條件約束參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1528">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1529">路由條件約束執行時機是出現符合傳入 URL 的項目，並將 URL 路徑語彙基元化成路由值時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1529">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1530">路由條件約束通常會透過路由範本檢查相關聯的路由值，並對是否可接受值做出是/否決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1530">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1531">某些路由條件約束會使用路由值以外的資料，以考慮是否可以路由要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1531">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1532">例如，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> 可以依據其 HTTP 指令動詞接受或拒絕要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1532">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1533">條件約束可用於路由要求和連結產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1533">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1534">請勿針對 **輸入驗證** 使用條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1534">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1535">如果針對 **輸入驗證** 使用條件約束，則無效的輸入會導致產生「404 - 找不到」回應，而不是「400 - 錯誤要求」與適當的錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1535">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1536">路由條件約束會用來 **釐清** 類似的路由，而不是用來驗證特定路由的輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1536">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1537">下表示範範例路由條件約束及其預期行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1537">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1538">constraint (條件約束)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1538">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1539">範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1539">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1540">範例相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1540">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1541">備註</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1541">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1542">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1542">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1543">符合任何整數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1543">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1544">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1544">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1545">符合 `true` 或 `false` (不區分大小寫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1545">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1546">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1546">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1547">符合非變異 `DateTime` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1547">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1548">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1548">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1549">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1549">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1550">符合非變異 `decimal` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1550">Matches a valid `decimal` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1551">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1551">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1552">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1552">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1553">符合非變異 `double` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1553">Matches a valid `double` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1554">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1554">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1555">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1555">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1556">符合非變異 `float` 文化特性中的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1556">Matches a valid `float` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1557">請參閱前面的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1557">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1558">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1558">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1559">符合有效的 `Guid` 值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1559">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1560">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1560">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1561">符合有效的 `long` 值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1561">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1562">字串必須至少有 4 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1562">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1563">字串不能超過 8 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1563">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1564">字串長度必須剛好是 12 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1564">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1565">字串長度必須至少有 8 個字元，但不能超過 16 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1565">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1566">整數值必須至少為 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1566">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1567">整數值不能超過 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1567">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1568">整數值必須至少為 18，但不能超過 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1568">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1569">字串必須包含一或多個字母字元 (`a`-`z`，不區分大小寫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1569">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1570">字串必須符合規則運算式 (請參閱有關定義規則運算式的提示)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1570">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1571">用來強制執行在 URL 產生期間呈現非參數值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1571">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1572">以冒號分隔的多個條件約束，可以套用至單一參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1572">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1573">例如，下列條件約束會將參數限制在 1 或更大的整數值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1573">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1574">確認 URL 可以轉換成 CLR 類型的路由條件約束 (例如 `int` 或 `DateTime`) 一律使用不因國別而異的文化特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1574">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1575">這些條件約束假設 URL 不可當地語系化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1575">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1576">架構提供的路由條件約束不會修改路由值中儲存的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1576">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1577">所有從 URL 剖析而來的路由值會儲存為字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1577">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1578">例如，`float` 條件約束會嘗試將路由值轉換成浮點數，但轉換的值只能用來確認它可以轉換成浮點數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1578">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1579">規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1579">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1580">ASP.NET Core 架構將 `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` 新增至規則運算式建構函式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1580">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1581">如需這些成員的說明，請參閱 <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1581">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1582">規則運算式使用的分隔符號和語彙基元，類似於路由和 C# 語言所使用的分隔符號和語彙基元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1582">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1583">規則運算式的語彙基元必須逸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1583">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1584">若要在路由中使用規則運算式 `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$`，運算式必須以字串中所提供的 `\` (單一反斜線) 字元作為 C# 原始程式檔中的 `\\` (雙反斜線) 字元，才能逸出 `\` 字串逸出字元 (除非使用[逐字字串常值](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string))。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1584">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1585">若要逸出路由參數分隔符號字元 (`{`、`}`、`[`、`]`)，請在運算式中使用雙字元 (`{{`、`}`、`[[`、`]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1585">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1586">下表顯示規則運算式和逸出的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1586">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1587">規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1587">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1588">逸出的規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1588">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1589">路由中所使用的規則運算式通常以插入號 (`^`) 字元開頭，並符合字串的開始位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1589">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1590">運算式通常以貨幣符號 (`$`) 字元結尾，並符合字串的結尾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1590">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1591">`^` 和 `$` 字元可確保規則運算式符合整個路由參數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1591">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1592">若不使用 `^` 與 `$` 字元，規則運算式會比對字串內的所有部分字串，這通常不是您想要的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1592">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1593">下表提供範例，並說明它們符合或無法符合的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1593">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1594">運算是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1594">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1595">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1595">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1596">比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1596">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1597">註解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1597">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
