| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1598">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1598">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1599">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1599">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1600">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1600">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1601">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1601">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1602">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1602">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1603">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1603">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1604">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1604">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1605">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1605">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1606">符合運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1606">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1607">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1607">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1608">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1608">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1609">不區分大小寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1609">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1610">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1610">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1611">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1611">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1612">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1612">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1613">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1613">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1614">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1614">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1615">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1615">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1616">如需規則運算式語法的詳細資訊，請參閱 [.NET Framework 規則運算式](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1616">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1617">若要將參數限制為一組已知的可能值，請使用規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1617">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1618">例如，`{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` 只會將 `action` 路由值與 `list`、`get` 或 `create` 相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1618">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1619">如果已傳入條件約束字典，字串 `^(list|get|create)$` 則是對等項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1619">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1620">已傳入條件約束字典 (未內嵌在範本內) 的條件約束，即使不符合其中一個已知的條件約束，也會被視為規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1620">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1621">自訂路由限制式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1621">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1622">除了內建的路由限制式之外，自訂路由限制式也可以透過實作 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 介面來建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1622">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1623"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 介面包含單一方法 `Match`，此方法會在滿足限制式時傳回 `true`，否則會傳回 `false`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1623">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1624">若要使用自訂 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>，路由限制式型別必須必須向應用程式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> (在應用程式的服務容器中) 註冊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1624">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1625"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 是一個目錄，它將路由限制式機碼對應到可驗證那些限制式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 實作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1625">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1626">更新應用程式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 時，可在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中於進行 [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) 呼叫時更新，或透過使用 `services.Configure<RouteOptions>` 直接設定 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> 來更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1626">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1627">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1627">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1628">限制式接著能以一般方式套用到路由 (使用註冊限制式型別時使用名稱)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1628">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1629">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1629">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1630">URL 產生參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1630">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1631">下列範例示範如何在指定路由值字典和 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection> 的情況下產生路由的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1631">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1632">在上述範例的結尾產生的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> 是 `/package/create/123`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1632">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1633">字典提供「追蹤套件路由」範本 `package/{operation}/{id}` 的 `operation` 和 `id` 路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1633">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1634">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用路由中介軟體](#use-routing-middleware)一節或[範例應用程式](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples)中的範例程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1634">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1635"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> 建構函式的第二個參數是「環境值」的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1635">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1636">環境值便於使用，因為它們會限制開發人員必須在要求內容中指定的值數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1636">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1637">目前要求的目前路由值被視為用於連結產生的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1637">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1638">在 ASP.NET Core MVC 應用程式 `HomeController` 的 `About` 動作中，您不需要指定控制器路由值以連結到 `Index` 動作&mdash;會使用 `Home` 的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1638">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1639">不符合參數的環境值會予以忽略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1639">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1640">當明確提供的值覆寫環境值時，也會忽略環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1640">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1641">URL 中的比對是從左到右。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1641">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1642">明確提供但不符合路由區段的值會新增至查詢字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1642">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1643">下表顯示使用路由範本 `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` 時的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1643">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1644">環境值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1644">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1645">明確值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1645">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1646">結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1646">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1647">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1647">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1648">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1648">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1649">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1649">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1650">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1650">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1651">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1651">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1652">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1652">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1653">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1653">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1654">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1654">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1655">如果路由具有未對應至參數的預設值，且該值會明確提供，它必須符合預設值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1655">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1656">連結產生只有在提供了 `controller` 與 `action` 的相符值時，才會產生此路由的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1656">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1657">複雜區段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1657">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1658">複雜區段 (例如，`[Route("/x{token}y")]`) 會透過以非窮盡的方式，由右至左比對常值來處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1658">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1659">請參閱[此程式碼](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/v2.2.13/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)以了解如何比對複雜區段的詳細解釋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1659">See [this code](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/v2.2.13/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fb78a-1660">[程式法範例](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/v2.2.13/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)不是由 ASP.NET Core 使用，但它提供一個好的複雜區段解釋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb78a-1660">The [code sample](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/v2.2.13/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>

::: moniker-end
